1)
True Parents
<Prayer> May the infinite love, mercy, and compassion of the Father dwell upon all of heaven and earth.
Father, who has woven the sorrowful history of restoration, how many countless people have betrayed You, and how much effort have You put into embracing the rebellious humanity? We know that there has never been a time when there were people who acknowledged You as their Father, and that there has not been a single tribe that can be called Your true children who have fulfilled their duty of loyalty and filial piety before You.
In order to establish Israel, You sought out a family to represent, and through that family, You sought to establish Your tribes and nations. However, we know that the Israelite people have betrayed You countless times. Such is the sad history of the Father… Although You sought to greet joy with the Israelite people and to manifest it before all of heaven and earth, due to human error, Your will has not been fulfilled, and You have come forth with sorrow! We have now taken on the responsibility of serving You in this age.
Although You established the Israelite people as representatives in the past, we know that it is our responsibility and mission today to figure out how to serve You as a joyful Father, as You were saddened by their failure to fulfill their responsibilities. This nation does not know You, but we know that we must represent this nation.
On the morning of September 21, 1969, at the former headquarters church (Cheongpadong 1-ga).
8   True Parents
We, who have been called first, feel that we are the last hope that cannot be absent before heaven.
When we think that we have the responsibility today to unite the hearts of countless nations scattered all around and to resemble Your heart, we feel even more the historical responsibility that no one has thought of or could fulfill throughout history. Although we may seem inadequate and insignificant, we must become the warriors of unification who realize that our fate is tied to the sorrow of history.
Father, today is September 21, the third Sabbath of this month. What do Your children scattered across the nation long for this morning? Please do not let us forget that we must fulfill our duty regarding the path of restoration that You have left behind. We know that we must not be the losers in this fight, but must become the princes of victory. Even if we have qualified for personal victory, we know that we still have the mission to fight to establish families. After establishing such families, we must face the arduous path of restoring tribes, nations, and the world.
We know that no matter how much effort and loyalty we put into overcoming such a hill, it is a hill that is difficult to cross, a hill that follows with sorrow, pain, and death. Father, please always be with us. You have labored for 6,000 years to help us cross this path. You have fought for 6,000 years and endured for 6,000 years. If this long and tedious path were to be entrusted to each of us today, who could bear it, and who could go forth with the dignity of being Your children? Knowing that there is not a single person who could, You have still endured until now, unable to abandon humanity. In the sorrowful journey of fighting and on the rugged path, You have overcome all things! We must become those who can praise Your holiness.
9 
We, who have been called into Your presence, have humbled ourselves before Your command, so we must become those who can ask You to command us as You wish. We wish to offer this body as the true substance of the offering You desire, so please accept us as Your true sons and daughters.
Let us know that we must become sons and daughters not just in words but in substance. We have learned through the principle that we cannot participate in that place without having the feeling of being one life, with Your bones connected and Your flesh intertwined. Therefore, we must become children who receive grafting from You. We must truly realize how much You have labored until now to graft us, who have not been able to escape the ties of the enemy's bloodline.
Father, please look down upon Your children gathered here at this time. We are orphans. Even when we look around, we have not yet met a single person with whom we can unite our hearts and hold hands to plead. Not only have we not met such a person, but we have not even known them, so now we can only turn to You, adjusting our collars and calling You Father, and we ask that You allow us to praise Your holiness. Not just in name, but let us become those who long for You based on substantial reality, and let us be able to follow Your path eternally and unceasingly. We must become those who truly thank You for the grace of being able to embrace the love of the Father in glory.
Father! When we reflect on the past, we find that we have no merit to call upon You. We have no record of good deeds that can connect us to You. Therefore, let us be able to thank You every time we stand in a position where we feel that.
Today, we must understand the sorrowful circumstances of the Father who has come to find this one nation, beyond all humanity, beyond countless nations. Gather us, who are chased and oppressed before this poor nation that has nothing to eat and is naked, and let us truly comfort Your sorrowful heart that demands the dignity of a son.
We must recognize the Father who stands in such a position, and we must become true sons and daughters who can comfort Your sorrowful heart by resembling Your strong power and strong appearance. Even though we should be those who must do so, we find ourselves in a pitiful position where we cannot help but ask for strength before You once again. Because human history has been like this, we cannot escape this connection as descendants of humanity, so we must earnestly appeal to You to have compassion on us once more.
We have entrusted all of our lives and existence to You, so please align us with Your will. Looking forward to the time when we can praise You before all people in glory, we earnestly hope and wish that we can endure and overcome all difficulties.
Now, please open all the doors of our hearts. Let us open our hearts so that You may come to us. When You call us, may we be able to respond and answer at any time, day or night. Just as Moses' staff was raised before him to part the Red Sea, let us be those who can discern direction and move forward as the staff raised before You.
Until now, we have made too many excuses in our past lives. Please forgive us for being too calculating and too comparative. Let us discover ourselves, who have not been able to struggle to become one with You in Your embrace, in Your mercy, and in Your love, and in what You desire. We earnestly hope and wish that You will forgive our past where we could not become such.
Please look down upon Your children gathered here at this time. Allow us to recognize how precious this time is. Let us know that this is the time to devote ourselves to You, to put our hearts into You, and to worship You. We earnestly hope and wish for this. Today, on behalf of countless nations, the children of unification have bowed down before You, so let them be remembered deeply in Your heart, and let them be children who fulfill the responsibilities of priests offering atonement for the sins of all humanity in the place aligned with Your providence, and let the church also fulfill such responsibilities. Please guide Your young sons and daughters who gather there to inherit Your will and Your holy ideals. May this become a foundation of victory and a point of hope.
How much have You despaired over humanity and how much have You grieved? We have realized how great the hope You desired in Your sorrowful heart is, so let us become dutiful sons and daughters who strive to comfort the Father who has been in such a position.
At this time, there are Your children from various places in South Korea who are looking toward this place, devoting their hearts and bodies to worship and pledging their loyalty before You, so please visit that place and bestow uniform grace upon them, and grant them the privilege of participating in the hope of tomorrow.
Father! Please be with Your countless children scattered across the world. They long for Korea as their homeland and are struggling to fulfill their responsibilities with a heart full of longing. Therefore, You must surely be with them. We, who are at the headquarters, must never become those who owe them. We know that we cannot maintain our dignity before anyone while in debt, so let us become Your sons and daughters who pledge to not be ashamed before them.
Although we may be lacking in everything externally, let us have the privileged authority to love You that we cannot yield to anyone, so that we may become a flower blooming amidst all the hardships of this nation and the pride of Korea. Thus, let us become the fragrance of life that can bring joy to Your heart, and let that glorious foundation become an eternal resting place.
Please bestow Your mercy upon countless nations, and as many of Your children face the difficult path of seeking You in the future, please gather the paths of indemnity and grant them the day when they can meet You in a place of joy that pleases You.
We have entrusted this day to You, so from morning to evening, please allow us to make progress in accordance with Your guiding will. We earnestly hope and wish that this month and this year may be established as a month of victory and a year of victory in accordance with Your will before the entire nation. We earnestly hope that Your glory may be revealed over the remaining days, and we pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
<Words> We know that the center of God's restoration history is not the world, nor any nation, nor any specific tribe or people. Before there can be a nation that God can be with, there must be a people that can represent that nation. For such a people to exist, there must be a tribe that can be central to that people, and for there to be a tribe, there must be a family, and for that family to exist, there must be parents. In order to bring about these parents, God has been working on the providence of individual restoration until now. Ultimately, the conclusion of everything is found in parents.
True Parents are the starting point of the restoration providence.
When we look at the past and present of history, there have been many large and small nations and numerous small peoples. There have also been countless families of religious people. However, those nations have not become the nations that God seeks, those peoples have not become the peoples that God seeks, and those families have not become the families that God seeks. All those families, peoples, and nations have passed away.
13 
We know that the restoration providence that has been carried out until now is to establish a family that can remain forever within God's will, and through that family, to establish a tribe, a people, and a nation that can remain forever. You must understand that this is the history of God's labor until now, seeking a day when He can love one family in place of all.
Then, even if a nation, a people, and a family have been established, what determines a standard that makes one forget all the labor that has been put into restoring the nation, people, and family is not the family, nor any brother, but parents. Unless the standard of true ancestors of humanity is determined here, the fruits of God's love cannot be borne. Furthermore, the struggles that God has fought until now cannot be concluded, nor can the highest victory be assured. The point of God's desires that He has wished for until now also cannot be determined. We must understand that True Parents are the point from which we can see a new beginning in establishing families centered on God's love.
Then, who should originally stand in such a position? It should be Adam and Eve before the Fall. God's desire, when viewed from the perspective of Adam and Eve, was not only for Adam as an individual or Eve as an individual, but more so, it was to determine the position of one set of parents centered on those two. That is God's ideal of creation and God's purpose of creation.
Then, what is the position that can be the origin of the hope for the bridegroom? It is the position of Adam and Eve.
This is a place where we become one. The Adam and Eve who grew up like this were meant to be bound together in one love, forming the starting point where they could love each other. This was the first place that humanity's ancestors were to establish. If, from such a place, centered on God's love, they had achieved an inseparable love that no one could break apart, the true parents of humanity would undoubtedly have started from here. However, we must understand that due to humanity's failure to align with the standards that God desired, this path was completely shattered. This was not due to external circumstances but rather an internal issue; it was entangled around love, and we know that correcting this is an exceedingly difficult problem, even if it requires unprecedented efforts in history.

Therefore, to resolve this in the future, numerous ethnic groups and nations that have split apart must come together. So how do we bind them together? We cannot bind them all at once. Thus, to form one nation, we need to establish one tribe that can represent the nation, one family that can represent the tribe, and one true person and participant who can represent the family, to externally bind everything that was divided back to its original state. In other words, we must establish two people, a man and a woman, who can represent the original parents of humanity instead of Adam and Eve. Through them, we must work backward toward the original standard, and you must understand that doing this is an exceedingly difficult task.

The Difficulty of the Restoration through Indemnity History
The history up to now has been a history of restoration through indemnity. In this history of restoration through indemnity, countless families and tribes have been mobilized, and numerous nations have passed through. However, at no time has any family, tribe, nation, or country ever aligned with God's will. They have always set conditions that made God sorrowful and have always produced results that made God despair. Therefore, the sorrow of God, who has dealt with countless families and tribes, countless nations and countries, remains until now. You must understand that the question of when these sorrowful stories can be resolved is an exceedingly difficult problem on the path of restoration.

Then, when we look at the numerous countries spread across the world, if there is a country that God desires to find, what kind of country would that be? What kind of nation could represent that country, what kind of tribe could organize that nation, and if there is one family that could form that tribe, what kind of family would that be? When we think from God's perspective, this is not a simple issue.

Historically, humanity has formed an inseparable blood relationship with Satan, making it impossible to separate from Satan. This is a bond that cannot be severed, and even if severed, it will be reestablished. Humanity is in such a fate. We must understand how exceedingly difficult it is to determine a family standard that can align humanity, which is under the realm of death, with God. Even if a national standard is established, finding a tribe that God can establish within that nation, finding a family that God can establish within that tribe, and finding the standard of the true parents of humanity who can represent God within that family in this fallen world is incredibly difficult.

Today, there are many countries that bear the name of Christianity and are within the Christian realm. There are also numerous tribes and families. However, the standard that God can say, "This is the family and nation I have established," is far removed from the current situation.

When we consider our habitual lives, we might say that the Republic of Korea stands in a position to be blessed before heaven, but it is difficult to assert that it is a blessed nation. Today, all nations stand in such a position. There are many countries on this earth, but they are very far from the heart of the Father who is seeking one nation as a standard. In other words, there is a significant distance between the lofty and precious work of God's holy creation and the stage of the wicked, realistic world.

So who will bridge that distance? Who will indemnify this? This is the problem. From God's side, resolving this issue must be a great concern. It cannot simply be filled. There must be a presentation of indemnity offerings on behalf of numerous ethnic groups and nations to overcome this. However, can those nations and ethnic groups suggest conditions that can indemnify everything? They cannot. Then who must do it? God must do it. God must present the conditions of indemnity before them to shorten and fill that distance. This struggle has been the history of the providence of restoration for 6,000 years. You must understand this.

Therefore, even if you establish a specific nation that God desires, you must recognize that there has been a historical indemnity of 6,000 years. Even if there is a nation equipped with such indemnity content, when we consider the standard at the time of its establishment and the duration that nation will take, whether it is 10 years or 20 years, or until the will is fulfilled, we must see that it is not possible to go forward united. Just as humanity has repeatedly failed in the historical process, that nation also cannot stand in a position to cooperate in bridging the historical distance with God. It may be possible for that nation to unite for a few years or months under certain circumstances, but to remain united for decades is exceedingly difficult. Therefore, even if it is a nation established by God, if that nation cannot align its period with God's will, it will completely perish.

The Intention to Find True Parents
So how have we sustained the fate of such a nation that is bound to perish? We have made a specific ethnic group the center to bridge the distance of that nation. If that ethnic group cannot bridge it, we have made a specific tribe within that ethnic group, for example, the Kim clan or the Park clan, bridge the distance that the ethnic group could not. However, if that tribe cannot fulfill its responsibility in bridging the distance with the nation that can represent God's will, we have made a specific family within that tribe bridge the distance that the tribe could not. Therefore, we must establish a specific family that can take on the responsibility of the tribe. And when that family cannot fulfill its responsibility, it must leave behind a standard that can extend that responsibility. So what is that standard that must be left behind? It is standing in the position of parents.

What is the ultimate purpose of God in carrying out the history of restoration until now? It is in true parents. The demand for true parents is to represent true families, the demand for true families is to represent true tribes, and the demand for true tribes is to represent true nations, true countries, and true worlds. This is how it develops.

If we look at it in reverse, to represent the world, a nation must be offered as an offering; to represent a nation, an ethnic group must be offered; to represent an ethnic group, a specific tribe must be offered; to represent that tribe, a specific family must be offered; and at the center of that family, a specific representative must be offered. Ultimately, it all culminates in parents.

Therefore, these parents can be the motive of history, the starting point of the formation of all nations, and the origin of all ethnic organization. That is why God cannot help but weave the history of restoration around parents who can be that origin.

Even if a nation and ethnic group are lost, if a family centered on the standard of true parents stands on a solid foundation, that family can reorganize the tribe, nation, and country. Therefore, even if everything is lost, the standard that can reorganize such content, in other words, the place that can be the starting point of humanity's hope, is precisely the place of true parents. You must understand this point.

Originally, Adam and Eve were to become the eternal, unchanging parents of the family, forming tribes, nations, and the world. However, because Adam and Eve fell, they could not achieve this, and you must understand that the 6,000 years of history until now has been an attempt to reorganize this from a new angle.

Who came to conclude this mission? It was Jesus Christ. What did Jesus Christ represent? He came representing the content of indemnity, representing the world, the nation, and also representing the ethnic group, tribe, and family. Jesus came as the center and representative of the whole, yet the Israelites did not recognize Jesus as such.

No one believed him as the representative of the nation, nor as the representative of the ethnic group, nor even as the representative of a family. However, God sent Jesus to establish him as the representative of the whole and the center of the whole. We must understand how great the difficulty was for Jesus, who could not have the environment to fulfill such a mission.

The Desire of Jesus
What Jesus desired was one nation, one ethnic group, one tribe, and one family. And he longed for true parents who could be the origin of that family. However, in determining true parents, one woman became an issue.

In finding that woman, it could not simply be a matter of drawing her up. Normally, a man can meet a woman at any time, but Jesus could not freely meet a woman due to vertical and horizontal environments. To meet that woman, Jesus had to establish the standard of a national representative, the standard of an ethnic representative, and the standard of a tribal and familial representative. He had to set all conditions that could align with the content of the providence of the 4,000 years of history until that time, and without establishing the condition of having completely indemnified this, Jesus could not meet a bride. You must understand this fact.

From the Bible, we can see that Jesus came as the bridegroom, so there must be a bride before him. However, that bride must not appear merely as a woman before a man on a flat and horizontal standard. She must stand before the standard that represents a nation, represents an ethnic group, represents a tribe, and represents numerous families centered on that tribe.

Then, what should such a representative woman be like? From the position of a daughter, she must be the daughter of daughters. Also, from the position of a wife, she must be the wife of wives, and among numerous mothers, she must be the one who can represent God's heart as a mother. 

So, was there such a woman among the Israelites? There was not. Therefore, when we reflect on the path that Jesus walked, the more than 30 years of life he lived on this earth, that path was to find a woman who could indemnify the sins of humanity along with Jesus, and that was a significant issue.

Furthermore, what kind of woman should that be? She must be a woman who can align with God's will based on historical background. Otherwise, it cannot be. She must have the historical background that is indispensable before the Israelite people or the nation of Israel.

Moreover, that woman must have the content to represent a nation, represent an ethnic group, represent numerous families, and represent numerous women. Without determining that, we cannot surpass the standard of restoration through indemnity. In other words, we cannot determine the standard of parents, who are the center of the whole. You must clearly understand this fact.

The history up to now has been a history of restoration through indemnity. This history is not a joyful history but a sorrowful one. In this sorrowful history, numerous nations are entangled, and countless ethnic groups and tribes, as well as many Israelite families, are entangled.

Because of the result of this history woven with sorrow, the woman who can represent all of this must not be an ordinary woman. She must be a woman who possesses specific content and has made a resolution to take on that responsibility. In other words, she must be a woman who has the specific content to represent numerous nations, numerous tribes, and numerous families in her heart.

And that woman must unite with Jesus, who comes representing all historical men with such resolution and self. This means that she must believe in Jesus, who comes as a man who can represent a nation, represent an ethnic group, represent a tribe, and represent a family, and she must become one with him. Without establishing such a standard, we cannot determine the relationship of true parents centered on the restored family.

The Mission of Christianity
In light of this, we can see that the 12 disciples and the 70 disciples chosen by Jesus did not fundamentally solve the internal issues. Jesus mobilized them to create a masculine framework that could represent the nation and the ethnic group. Thus, he sought to connect himself to a substantial entity based on that foundation. For this, he needed to represent many men who had historically failed and to present the representative figures of that time, which were the twelve disciples and the 70 disciples.

If the twelve disciples and the 70 disciples could completely unite with Jesus, all the failures of men who had not been indemnified throughout history would be indemnified. 

That is why Jesus had to create a horizontal foundation that could manage historical failures by completely uniting with them. He had to establish a solid, impregnable framework, determining a victorious foundation as a man that Satan could not attack. The ones who must fulfill the mission of that framework are the twelve disciples and the 70 disciples.

On this foundation, they must firmly stand and find the woman mentioned earlier to create the standard of motherhood. To do this, they had to go through a significant struggle, just as they had fought throughout history. The twelve disciples and the 70 disciples did not know that there were internal circumstances that necessitated this for Jesus.

Thus, Jesus never had this environmental foundation. He could not find a counterpart who could fulfill such a mission, nor could he communicate such internal matters.
Without finding even a single disciple, He spent over 30 years of His life and ultimately was nailed to the cross and died. Because Jesus died on the cross, if there is any sorrow, He must have had more sorrow than anyone else. God spent 4,000 years weaving history and sent Jesus to meet a certain time, yet fundamentally, everything God desired fell apart. Furthermore, even though Jesus came to establish a victorious foundation in the 4,000-year history woven by God through men, He had to leave without establishing it. You must understand how unfortunate that situation was for Jesus.

Jesus did not care about His own death. He was more saddened by the fact that the providence of God, which had been unfolding through men for 4,000 long years, would all come to nothing because of His death. He felt a deeper sorrow over the failure of God's providence than over His own suffering. You need to understand this heart of Jesus.

However, because Jesus was determined and resolved to once again restore the historical foundation, He boldly broke through the path of the cross, allowing Him to align with God's heart and spiritually restore His disciples. Through this, He was able to create a second fence, reorganizing the history of Christianity centered around men today. Thus, centered on spiritual standards, Christianity has developed through 2,000 years of countless martyrdom.

When we look at the history of Christianity, it should not be a vague ideological realm of a nation, but rather it must re-establish a specific nation that can completely resolve all internal issues that were not settled during Jesus' time. This path of indemnity remains. Therefore, in the end, a specific nation must become an issue.

So, what is that specific nation? Among many nations, it must be known that Korea should be that specific nation. The people of Korea must fulfill that mission. Among them, we who are in Korea must strive to fulfill that mission.

Blessed families must become the fence of True Parents. Today, when we look at the Unification Church, what should the 36, 72, and 124 blessed families who received blessings from 1960 do? You must understand this. These families must complete the mission of being a central fence with external standards that Jesus could not have during His lifetime. Thus, they must connect all the contents of indemnity that can represent the world, the nation, and even the ethnic and family levels, and take on the responsibility to connect a relative standard. This is the responsibility of the families blessed during the three years from 1960.

During Jesus' time, families did not even have the noun "blessing" nor did they go through that process. Therefore, the families that have gone through the standard of blessing now must become an external fence for all families, unlike that era.

From this perspective, today in Korea, there are many families that have established a connection with True Parents centered on the ideology of the Unification Church. There are over 800 blessed families so far; what should these families do? In those families, the men must become the absolute representatives of masculinity before the returning Lord and serve as a relative foundation that can connect the historical sorrow. Additionally, women must appear as representatives who can resolve the historical sorrow of their existence not having appeared in God's providence until now, as there has never been a time when women have stood equally before God's providence. 

The privilege of being able to appear in such a way has been granted because they are blessed families. Therefore, in relation to men, women must become an internal fence that represents all women and can indemnify all the vertical history woven from the past to the present, connecting it to the family.

Thus, if one family returns, all 800 families must return, and if that family comes out, the whole must be able to come out. In other words, even if one man and one woman return, that entire family must be connected before True Parents, and even when coming out centered on True Parents, that entire family must stand at the standard of a family that can represent the nation. Otherwise, complete indemnity and restoration cannot be achieved. You must understand this well.

From this perspective, the teacher must become the offering representing all men throughout the 6,000 years of history, and among offerings, He must be the highest offering. This position is not a specific personal position. It is not a position that represents only a certain family, tribe, or nation. He must be an offering representing the world and history.

Throughout history, many men have come and gone. God has worked through many men, from Abel to Noah, Abraham, Moses, John the Baptist, and Jesus, but the teacher must remain above them both internally and externally, as well as vertically and horizontally. When facing them, He must not stand in a shameful position. In other words, He must become a global fruit representing all men. You must understand that without standing in such a position, complete indemnity and restoration cannot be achieved.

So, what is the mission of the Unification Church centered on such a teacher? The Unification Church has a greater mission to unite with the teacher guiding the church than to develop the church itself. You must understand that the most important responsibility is to unite with the teacher rather than individual responsibilities. Without determining the standard to unite with the teacher, you cannot fulfill your own responsibilities.

Therefore, men must completely unite centered on the male teacher, and in that unity, their circumstances or positions, such as their families or environments, must not become issues. They must stand in a position of complete unity beyond all those environments.

In that united position, there can be no gaps. Nothing should be able to break through here. It must be a completely unified standard. Determining this standard is a serious matter that depends on whether you fulfill your responsibilities.

Also, women must completely unite centered on the female teacher. Women cannot stand alone as women; they must stand on the foundation centered on the mother. Therefore, women must completely unite with their mothers. Only then can they fulfill their responsibilities as women, so women must unite centered on their mothers.

The teacher's responsibility. Originally, history has been woven around the connection between men and women. Therefore, men and women must be connected at a single point. That connection must be centered on the content of True Parents, and True Parents must start from the origin of history. In other words, if history began centered on Adam and Eve, it would extend to the world of eternal results, but because this was disrupted, the origin of history must be recreated.

Thus, to recreate the origin of history, the history that has been laid out must be restored, and for that, a man and a woman must be connected centered on True Parents. Without that, we cannot transition to a new historical era. This is what the Unification Church must realistically do today. You must understand this.

Then, what is the teacher's responsibility guiding the Unification Church? It is to determine the connection of True Parents. This is an important mission that no one has thought of until now. Therefore, to determine this, what kind of woman must a woman be, and what kind of man must a man be? In other words, what kind of father must the teacher be, and what kind of mother must the mother be?

Without solving this issue, the problems of the nation, the world, and the heavenly realm cannot be resolved. Therefore, this issue becomes the most important issue. Without making a complete victory decision from here, everything will return to nothing, and God's providence will be extended again. Therefore, you must understand that this issue has been the standard for the internal struggle that has been ongoing since 1960.

The union of the two is not simple. It is not a simple matter for one man and one woman to meet and become one. All historical issues are at stake here.

When we look at the United States and Korea today, there are countless issues that cannot be reconciled between the two countries. Their cultures are different, their histories are different, and all social organizations are different. It is difficult for these different environments to simply become one. There are many reasons why they cannot unite. However, what is even more difficult is the issue of indemnity that is at stake, which is the issue of these two becoming one.

If there is a pitfall here, that pitfall will be deeper than any other pitfall, and if there is a mountain, that mountain will be higher than any other mountain. This cannot be seen from our flat perspective; it can only be seen from the perspective of the world of heart, which is a high mountain and a deep valley. How do we establish a standard that can become flat here? The time when that standard is established is when True Parents appear on this earth with their connections, and until then, history is a history of sorrow. We must understand that this path of indemnity exists in human history.

These are the people who have been set aside. Therefore, when they reach their 50s, they believe they have reached an age where they can dedicate everything to stepping onto the world stage and demonstrating their skills in their professional fields.

Wherever you go in famous places around the world, there are always Americans present. When you see people staying in tourist hotels, more than two-thirds of them are Americans. Looking at this, we can see that the U.S. will continue to hold the authority of a developed country in the future.

In the academic field, they build a foundation by accumulating skills to a certain standard domestically before moving onto the international stage. In the global academic community, they meet people related to their studies or refer to all the presentations made by others in the same field, experimenting with their research centered around the practical world stage. After that, they gather the results and play a significant role globally.

This is why a considerable amount of the national budget in the U.S. is allocated for foreign travel. However, this expense ultimately returns to the U.S. as invisible profits. When Americans return to their homeland, they do not come back empty-handed; they always bring back materials that can contribute to their professional fields.

For example, if a businessman is exploring markets in various countries, he will focus on that field and establish connections with the upper echelons of each country. In other words, if he is in the industrial sector, he will build relationships with the upper echelons of that country's industry.

They select a few important companies in that country and, after receiving briefings on the company’s details and operational methods, they understand the circumstances of that company. Since it is their area of expertise, they can quickly gauge the level of the company's products just by visiting a few factories. They listen to the company's briefings and assess what kind of auxiliary facilities need to be established based on the current production results to explore the market.

Because these experts travel around the world, the costs incurred are significant, but the gains are equally substantial. When they return to the U.S., they have undoubtedly laid the groundwork for deep, high, and broad positions globally. This is a movement to establish a solid foundation for the future of the U.S., beyond its current status. Observing this, one can infer that the U.S. will continue to maintain its authority as a developed country in the future.

Regarding American industrial technology, the teacher visited IBM factories and several other large factories in the U.S., but they were different from Korean factories in many aspects today. In Korea, factories are built tall, but in the U.S., they absolutely do not do that. Of course, in cities, there are multi-story factories, but the majority are single-story. They are built in harmony with the natural environment, without damaging it. Given the vast land and abundant materials, they prefer to build single-story structures.

No matter how famous a factory is, when you look at its exterior, it feels just like an ordinary factory. A renowned factory does not appear particularly impressive or special from the outside. However, once you enter, it is quite different. The internal facilities are all scientifically designed.

Americans are practical in this way. In creating culture, they focus on qualitative foundations rather than outward appearances. In the U.S., any factory has been simplified to quickly assimilate all materials relevant to its specialized field. Every factory is organized in such a way. Most of them are automated.

From this, we can see that the U.S. has reached a standard in future scientific civilization that no other country’s scientific technology can match, no matter how advanced it may be.

The Hoover Dam, constructed in the triangular area of Arizona, California, and Nevada, is the world’s number one multipurpose dam, built with an astonishing capital of $170 million. The area around the dam is a desert, and its expanse is immeasurable. Nevada is a desert area where atomic bombs were tested, and Arizona is a place frequently featured in western films.

The water from the river flows in from various regions and all drains into a corner of one area. Other places are blocked by mountain ranges, causing the water to flow in one direction. The river is about 170 meters wide, and judging by the mountains on both sides, it seems that the water was initially pooled. As the water continued to accumulate, the force of the water broke through the mountains, allowing it to flow, with a drop of 172 meters. Here, 720,000 kilowatts (kw) of electricity are generated per hour. It is impressive when you visit.

However, because the river is deep, the challenge was how to block the water and build the dam. The issue was how to divert the water elsewhere in order to block it. To solve this problem, they left the river as it was and drilled two large tunnels into the rock beside it, allowing all the river water to flow through those tunnels. After draining the river, they proceeded with the dam construction.

The openings of those tunnels are enormous. Since they were drilled through rocky mountains, they could easily drain water, but they also connected iron pipes in the shape of water pipes to drain the water.

The size of those iron pipes is such that one piece would require 35 large trucks to transport. It is unimaginable. The bolts used to connect the pipes are also larger than one would expect. They installed such things in the tunnels and drained the water.

The teacher has traveled around 49 of the 50 states in the U.S., but the factory facilities did not seem that impressive. Yet, they can extract such heavy iron pipes all at once, which indicates how advanced the country's industrial technology is.

Furthermore, the amount of cement used to build the dam is enough to construct a major highway that crosses from San Francisco in the West to Washington in the East. Looking at this, it is incomparable to what is done in Korea or Japan.

The U.S. is a blessed country. 

When you look at the highways across the U.S., in urban areas, there are lanes up to 12 wide, but mostly there are 6 lanes. Traveling on such highways, you mostly pass through primeval forest areas. Wherever you go, you pass through primeval forests. In Korea, it is hard to encounter such primeval forest areas. You might find them in the deep valleys of Baekdu Mountain, but I have visited Jirisan and other nearby mountains, and there are no such primeval forests.

If you cut down and burn the trees in those primeval forest areas, it would create the best arable land. In the U.S., there are primeval forest areas everywhere you go. They have cut through those primeval forests and paved highways right through the middle. While Korea is currently paving the Gyeongbu Expressway, the U.S. does not do it that way. They must plant grass on both sides of the highway that is wider than the highway itself.

Thus, the width of the highway becomes more than double when you include the grassy areas on either side. The grass planted there is truly beautiful. There is grass in Korea, but the grass in the U.S. is finer. They have planted such fine grass along the highways. They do not just leave it; when it grows to a certain height in spring, they send in cars to mow and trim it. They have made it so well that even if you drive over it, not a speck of dust will stick to your car.

The cultural level of a country can be seen through its road infrastructure. Germany boasted about the Autobahn built just before World War II, but compared to American highways, it is nothing. Thus, just by looking at the roads, we can see that America has a high cultural level and is wealthy.

The population of the U.S. is 180 million, but you cannot feel that anywhere you go across the country. Of course, in places like New York, there are many high-rise buildings, but elsewhere, it is not the same. To travel from one city to another, you have to drive hundreds of miles. Even then, it is hard to find a city.

In rural areas, there are usually only a few houses, and they all farm using modern machinery. They do not use tools like hoes. Everything is mechanized. Therefore, even if one person farms, they can produce thousands of sacks. One household can have a farm so large that it seems endless. 

Because of this, although there are only a few farms in one region, the amount of crops produced in a year is incomparable to Korea. There is so much that they sometimes scatter it into the Pacific Ocean or distribute it in the mountains for wild animals like deer to eat. Observing this, one can see that America is truly a blessed country.

Japan's land is about twice the size of Korea, yet there are now 100 million people living there. If all the people in the world lived like those in Japan, the entire 3.2 billion population could fit into the U.S. 

Moreover, such a vast land has abundant resources. The oil production alone accounts for one-fifth of the world's oil production, and it has the world's best iron ore resources. It is a country rich in various resources that can be self-sufficient. After traveling through such a country and comparing it to Korea, I felt that Korea is indeed a lamentable place.

I have traveled from the U.S. to South America, Europe, and Southeast Asia, and I found that the common desire among the youth of every country is to visit the U.S. at least once.

The current state of American youth

When I compare my trip to the U.S. in 1965 with this year, 1969, one thing has changed. The social and cultural systems have not changed. So what has changed? When I went to the U.S. in 1965, there were not many hippies. I heard that there were hippies at some universities, but it was difficult to meet them. However, this time, just walking around the streets, I found them every 20 or 30 steps. There are all kinds of people among the hippies. Their behavior is extravagant. Regardless of what anyone says about them, they wander around the streets in all sorts of appearances, and when they are hungry, they go anywhere to find food.

But what they are seeking is the true essence of life. I could feel that the number of such people has increased significantly compared to four years ago. Berkeley University is world-renowned. It has produced 82 Nobel laureates, making it a prestigious university. Yet, when you enter its campus, it is bizarre.

Some of them are hanging from the tops of palm trees. I thought only boys would do such things, but girls do it too. They do as they please. The cowboy look from western movies is common. Some students are even just wearing underwear. Male and female students are engaging in all sorts of bizarre behavior on campus.

So why have they become this way? They have no hope. They have reached the highest level in many areas, so there is nothing in the world to envy. All the renowned scholars are in the U.S., and all the wealthy tycoons are also in the U.S. They have lived within that cultural background and have become accustomed to such lifestyles, which is why they do not find satisfaction there. This does not define the highest happiness of humanity. Thus, exotic religions are increasingly on the rise.

This will become a terrifying demon, more frightening than an atomic bomb, in determining the future of America. Therefore, how America manages this is the issue.

Currently, young people in America are taking a hallucinogen called LSD. This drug makes them feel like they are in a dream world. When they take opium, they feel like the world is coming in and out of them, and that the solar system is also coming in and out of their stomachs; it is the same with hallucinogens. Young people take these drugs to experience momentary sensations, but still, nothing remarkable happens. So now they want to return to primitive times and engage in all sorts of antics. The question is how to manage these issues in the future.

As I traveled across America, I felt that I absolutely do not want to live there. Furthermore, I believe that educating children in America is absolutely not a good idea. When you drive along the highways in America, you see high-end cars that you would never see in Korea. For example, if a new model comes out in 1969, everyone wants to buy that car. Even students compete to drive those cars. If you do not drive such a car, you cannot find a girlfriend or boyfriend to date.

The problems in America

As this happens, those who cannot keep up will inevitably react. Because of such an environment, on one hand, culture and science have developed, and they benefit from that, but on the other hand, they have entered a period conducive to movements that undermine America. This is why the Communist Party is currently conducting extensive propaganda within the U.S.

If one thinks that communism will disappear in the U.S. just because America is withdrawing from the Vietnam War, that is an absolutely mistaken belief. Even in broad daylight, the communists hold microphones in parks and promote communism. They also consider acts of terrorism as normal. The U.S. is currently in a favorable environment for communist infiltration. President Nixon's policy of withdrawing from Vietnam may have been established due to some underlying circumstances in the country, but implementing that policy will not add any positive value to America.

When I asked a certain individual if America could defend itself if it became isolated in the Pacific, they said it could. However, that is absolutely not true. Right next to them is Cuba, which has become communist. If Mexico also becomes communist, wouldn’t we see a repeat of the Vietnam War? This is a question that can be considered logically. Just wait a few years. Such operations will undoubtedly emerge. At that time, Cuba will not be the only issue. It will definitely revolve around the continent, and if a war similar to the Vietnam War breaks out, what will America do then?
People who are currently implementing policies in the United States are concerned about the future of America. Everyone living in the U.S. is deeply influenced by individualism. This ideology is particularly prevalent among the younger generation in American society. How can we overcome this? This is a problem that America must address in the future. Based on this reality, the U.S. must continue to prepare for what lies ahead.

Currently, if you visit the landmarks of advanced European countries like the UK or France, as well as Germany or Italy, which established a new system after World War II, you will see many beggars. A country with many beggars is a country that is failing.

However, if you visit parks or landmarks in America, you will find that there are no people walking alone. While there are couples strolling together, there are no individuals looking for something. It is hard to even see that. In contrast, there are many people begging in England. In France, and especially in Italy, if you visit public parks, you will see a multitude of such individuals.

From this, we can gauge the general living standards of those countries. Additionally, by observing the roads and the traffic order in those countries, we can generally infer their cultural level.

Until now, the UK has played a leading role in creating Western civilization, but now it looks up to America. When you ask students, they all express a desire to go to America. This is true for France and Germany as well. Everyone is yearning for America.

However, if this is the state of the America they admire, what will happen to the younger generations around the world in the future? This is a global issue. Thus, the youth problem has become a significant concern today.

God will govern based on Eastern thought.

What have you felt while traveling around the world? What I have felt while visiting countries like America is that I do not want to live in such places. I also realized that our Korea possesses a unique cultural background as a unified single ethnic group with a national spirit that does not lag behind any other nation.

When we look at the Korean people, we generally find that they lack independence and autonomy. This is not the case for Europeans or Americans. No matter how wealthy a person is, once they turn 18, their father will no longer cover their tuition fees. They consider it shameful to pay for their children's education. While this is essential for developing individuality and establishing an independent foundation, it hinders the inheritance of tradition. It becomes difficult to pass on the unique thoughts of that country or the spirit of patriotism. Everyone is focused on themselves, proposing something new.

When you travel the world, you will find that America has established itself in almost every field. Whether in science or any other area, Americans occupy the top positions globally. Therefore, no matter how hard Europeans study and research, they are treated like ragged bundles. They try to strengthen their independent ideas through education to secure the best positions within American society, but Americans have already done that. Their efforts are ultimately just following what others have done.

Their educational methods are centered on instilling strong independent thoughts. As a result, rather than absolutely conforming to a scholar's theory, they tend to view everything from a critical perspective. This is why they cannot inherit unique traditional thoughts. This is a significant issue within the current American education system.

In this regard, we can see how valuable Eastern thought is. In the East, children live centered around their parents until they establish themselves. In other words, as a member of society, one does not leave their parents until they are qualified to have a solid foundation. In this respect, the historical background of Eastern families, social systems, and ethical systems differs from that of the U.S.

While this has been a significant hindrance to the advancement of scientific civilization, it has served as an absolute foundation in the pursuit of personal perfection. Therefore, in terms of family, social systems, or human relationships, the East is more advanced than Western societies. This can be felt anywhere.

Considering this internal culture, we can clearly see that God must govern based on Eastern culture rather than Western culture.

Next, while reflecting on the world, I have felt one more thing. What is it? Western civilization is Christian civilization, but currently, America is adding a new scientific civilization while simultaneously refuting Christian civilization, meaning it exists within the realm of Christian civilization while opposing it. This is due to the shortcomings of religion. Religion centers on the standards of the old era, absolutizing them, and does not allow any gaps for the establishment of new cultures. It desires that the standards remain the same today and a thousand years from now. This does not fit with a developing world. Therefore, people who have continued historical traditions based on a religious background and those who have encountered new social ideologies and developed new religious thoughts are all diverging in different directions.

Until now, how has religion been treated in America? Fifty years ago, the unique thoughts of Christianity were absolutized. However, this began to change about 30 or 40 years ago. With rapidly changing cultures and social conditions, religion should have transformed to align with new trends, but it has not been able to do so, leading to problems. 

When I traveled through the Arab countries of the Islamic cultural sphere, I also found that new revolutionary energies were sprouting there.

What should our Unification Church do in the future? This is the question. Our church must establish a religious system based on an ideology that can encompass new cultures of the 21st century, 30th century, and even the 100th century. As the one responsible for our church, I cannot help but worry about what foundation we will establish this upon.

What is the traditional thought that remains in Christianity? It is about doing good while sacrificing oneself. Christianity has established a tradition of achieving goals through self-sacrifice. While looking to the future, it has maintained a perspective of hope rather than a position of achieving that hope.

Those who have hope will inevitably remain through the course of history. However, our goal is not a hopeful standard but the completion of the substance of hope. The important issue is how we will set such a standard and make it our traditional thought.

In the future, there will come a time when we cannot help but raise the torch of revolution in any society or world. We must prepare a foundation that can surpass that era. But what will we use to prepare it? It is the family. It is the family centered on ideal love. We absolutize this. This cannot be revolutionized in any social system or in any era.

Therefore, centered on such families, when we only preach the most ideal content that can replace human history and surpass the phenomena of society, this will remain as an eternal ideology. When viewed in this light, we can see that our intention will become the focal point of issues in any historical era to come.

The ideal family we advocate, in other words, a family centered on God’s creation ideal, will become a family that can replace history, a family that can replace the era, and a family that can replace the future. The history and culture up until now have been pursued with the future's purpose in mind. They have formed culture from a pursuing standpoint.

In that world, there will be various ideologies and theories, but what should we do in the future? We should not pursue the future; rather, we must enable the future to pursue the past. We must establish an absolute standard for one aspect of the past. Without firmly establishing such a foundation, world unification is impossible. Do you understand what I am saying?

How will we set that standard that will not change even after a thousand or ten thousand years? Even if people of the future devote all their sincerity and efforts centered on an absolute standard of the past, they will find it insufficient to reach it, while being compelled to hold onto the belief that they must absolutely adhere to it. If that is the case, the world will automatically unify around that standard.

In this regard, there can be no absolute unity in the phenomenal world centered on the dialectics of materialism of communism. The very idea of achieving unity through struggle is a logical contradiction. They may hope for the future and pursue unity, but they cannot achieve a unified world through such methods.

So what will be the core ideology that becomes the historical, epochal, and future center? In other words, what will be the center of a universal thought that can be the historical fruit, the epochal center, and the future source? It is the true man and the true woman. Then what will be the lifestyle of the true man and true woman? It is living meaningfully for the world. Their love for each other is love for the world, and having children is to create motives to love the world even more.

This is the ideology we are currently advocating. Whether you are aware of this in detail or not, from my perspective, it is an automatic conclusion that history must be clarified based on that standard, whether viewed through the horizontal three-dimensional world or the vertical historical narrative.

The question is us.

Then, where should we place the standard of happiness and success in our pursuit of a happy path? Should we place it in knowledge? In science? No. It is a matter of heart. No matter how much authority a leader of a nation has to control that country, where is the source of that person's happiness? It is in the family. When we sing of family peace above all else and sing of family happiness above all else, that is when we are the happiest.

Therefore, the authority of the family I possess, the feelings I have about my family, and the entire system of the family cannot be obtained through anything else. It cannot be obtained through academic means. Everyone absolutizes this and desires it so much that they would dedicate their lives for it. When we firmly grasp this, we can move the world.

From that perspective, when we view God's providence, Jesus is the bridegroom before humanity, and those who believe in Jesus are the bride, which is the highest standard in a relative relationship. I have felt this while traveling around various countries.

We must become people who have established such families and create one nation, one world. But what kind of nation will we create? It would be problematic to create a nation like those in the current world. We must establish a world centered on the Creator, the Absolute, with love, where our families are united in a three-dimensional sense. We must strive until families become one, not individuals.

This movement is currently taking place in a modest form on the Korean Peninsula in Asia, but when it has woven itself into human history and has established a position in the past, present, and future, it will surely become a global event.

Then what will be the standard of personality in such an era? It must be based on the heart centered on God's principles of creation. And the purpose must be global. However, it should not end with being global. While communism has aimed for world domination until now, they have already split into two. This means they have already seen the end and are falling apart. They cannot charge forward toward a world beyond that. The same goes for the democratic world.

Where there is heaven, there will be earth, and where there is heaven and earth, there will be a man and a woman symbolizing this. The emotional standard that can unite this in a three-dimensional sense is the family. This family can penetrate any process as an absolute standard for the purpose world. From there, a new history, a new world, and a new foundation for the universe will be established. When we think about this, the question is us.

When we need to find what we have lost.

Now, the communist world and the democratic world have clashed, right? But this is merely a passing scene. From now on, they will separate within themselves. Democracy will separate within itself, and communism will separate within itself. When they collapse, they will not just fall apart. They must inevitably clash.

Democracy has claimed peace while clashing with its own separated parts. The era of fighting to dominate the world centered around one's own nation has now passed.

However, communists do not think that way. They aim to make the world theirs centered on themselves, so ultimately, they will struggle against the world. The process of struggle remains. In their pursuit of world domination, they maintain an ideological consciousness centered on themselves, which means they will continue to fight against the world as long as that ideology remains. When the time comes for them to separate and fight among themselves, they will perish. The day China and the Soviet Union clash is the day they will fall. On that day, the world will become ours.

Today, the world cannot determine the direction of culture or the direction of global trends. It is not moving based on any political theory proposed by scholars. It is not moving based on any ideology. When searching for the world based on any perspective, they ultimately find that they have lost everything. In countries like America, where individualism is rampant, they have lost their parents, their spouses, and their children. Having lost everything, what should they do? They must find it again. We have now entered a stage where such a movement will occur.

God's providence is mysterious. Ultimately, after losing everything, they will realize that what they have lost is more precious than what they currently possess. At that point, they will turn back.

Considering the will of God, who chose our people in a corner of Asia as a chosen people to create such an era, we are not a people to despair. Knowing this underlying connection, we must march forward with a hopeful tomorrow, raising the flag of new historical creation. A majestic era has come before us.

What will you become in the future? Will you succeed and become a doctor? What will you achieve by becoming a doctor? Will that fulfill the purpose of humanity?
is not a place where one would want to live. 

The essence of life is not found in grand spectacles but in the simple joys of existence, which we often overlook. In Korea, we have a unique blend of nature and culture that nurtures our spirit and well-being. 

Korea is a small country, but it is rich in natural beauty and resources. The mountains, rivers, and climate all contribute to a quality of life that is hard to find elsewhere. The air is fresh, the water is pure, and the land is fertile. This is a blessing that we should cherish and protect. 

As we move forward, we must remember the importance of our heritage and the values that have shaped our identity. We are at a crossroads where we can either embrace our potential or allow it to slip away. The future of our nation depends on our ability to recognize and cultivate the gifts we have been given. 

Let us strive to create a society that values not just material wealth but also the richness of our spiritual and cultural heritage. In doing so, we can build a brighter future for ourselves and generations to come.
to be continued...
Will you create a world that can digest the eternal motivation for life and the source of power? Let us all think about it together. It is possible. If you pull one string, it can be pulled to that mountainous area or to that sea; if the hearts of the people of the world are all in unison—whether it is east, west, south, or north, up or down—if there is one ideology or thought that can transcend space and time in all directions, how joyful would that be? The teacher thinks so. Think about what will happen on the day such an ideology or thought emerges. That day will be the best day in history. The teacher believes that such a day will come.

Everyone, do people in the world say there is a God or not? They say there isn't. Do you think there is one or not? "I think there is." If you enter a place where lightning strikes and the ground splits, you might not be so sure. Is that so? (Laughter) Have you seen God? Is He really there? Answer vividly! "Yes, He is."

If God exists, and if people say there is no God, but in reality, God is there, lifting the earth and lowering the heavens, what would happen if the universe were to rise and fall just twice? People would cry out, "Oh my God!" whether it rises or falls. Wouldn't they?

And if there were a great transformation, where God appeared in the world for all of humanity to see and held a feast, what would happen? People would gather, wondering who God's bride might be, creating a commotion. Would you want to see God's bride or not? Even if told not to look, everyone would gather to see. Even the children would crawl up from their mothers' arms, saying, "Me too, me too." That is how it would be. If God got married and had a son, and if that son appeared here today, would you want to see him or not? What about you? "I want to see him."

Ultimately, all the problems in the human world cannot be solved by humans alone. While the world was nervously watching Apollo 11, we must create a moment in history where we can joyfully and beautifully smile, rather than just nervously watching. What kind of moment is that? It is the moment when all the issues regarding God that I speak of are resolved. So how do we resolve those issues? We must recognize that we need to make greater sacrifices than those made to launch Apollo 11, when the hearts of all humanity united.

Which is easier, launching Apollo 11 or witnessing God’s feast, as mentioned earlier? Is it easier to launch Apollo or to see God’s feast? It is easier to launch Apollo. So what kind of people are we? We are people who want to make it possible for God to hold a feast. Since I said that first, I will be the first to be able to do so. We are people who want to live with that kind of heart. Are we just saying we believe in Jesus to go to heaven? How do we know if we will go to heaven or hell? We will only know when we go.

When I went to America, I decided in front of the White House to meet again in twenty years. With just a fist, what could I believe in? But from now on, I will prepare steadily. As the first operation, I plan to lay the groundwork in Korea and Japan. Once we move to the second phase of the operation, we will go to America. For that time, you may not know well, but right now in America, we are focusing on laying the internal groundwork.

Until now, Westerners have regarded Korea, a country in Asia, as trash. However, in this land of Korea, there is an ideological background that can present the issues of building a new cultural world. Here, we must prepare an absolute origin that cannot be denied in any future world by centering our hearts and transcending historical eras. We should try to roll forward centered around this Korean Peninsula. To do that, you must become the rails from now on. Do you have the confidence to be the rails? Do you have the confidence to endure even if you roll and slide a thousand or ten thousand times? "Yes." If you have confidence, let’s give it a try. Ladies, do you have confidence? "Yes."

What will you do after graduating from university? Will you become a 20,000-won salaryman? That is too trivial to even wipe your nose with. So you will become a 20,000-won salaryman and sell yourself for a few thousand won? Raise your hand if you want to be a salaryman. Now, raise your hand if you don’t want to be one. What is this? If you don’t want to be a salaryman, what will you do? If you don’t want to be a salaryman, you must become the owner, right? You must be the owner.

Now, I have cut off all those thoughts, but in the past, I thought there was nothing I couldn’t do. In fact, that was true. Whether it was track and field or any sport, I never failed to place in the top three. My physical strength was not inferior to anyone else’s, but it was the same with anything I did. On the days when I took on a task, I was someone who disliked even coming in second. I hated following what others did.

That is why, even when I read literary works like novels, if there is a good phrase, I would erase it with a pencil. This guy wrote it before I did…. (Laughter) I can sit for three hundred sixty days and write a long novel every day without reading any novels. Do you understand what I mean?

When I ended up in prison, I was good at befriending the prison guards. With just a few words, I would become friends quickly. Then, sitting there, I would analyze the psychology of each person who came in, saying, "This person looks like this, so he will turn out like that," and "That person looks like that, so he will end up like this."

When I talk, at first, you may not know what I mean and find it uninteresting, but as I speak more engagingly, you become interested and forget to eat. When I align with the spiritual waves, your eyes turn upside down. That’s how rumors about holiness and such started. My words have a broad wavelength in a three-dimensional sense rather than a horizontal one.

Who taught us our principles? How did it happen? God taught us everything. That is why anyone can receive it. If you pray before God and align with the spiritual waves, you can receive it all.

You may not realize how many times God has been with us. Now, I drive a car and hear that no one in South Korea envies me, but in the past, when I was hungry, God fed me. Suddenly, a lady would appear on the street in white clothes, and if it was evening, she would prepare dinner for me. It was pitiful. If I made a mistake then, it would have been a big deal. But I couldn’t help it if I was someone. I have had many such histories.

You are following the teacher now, and you come to our church, but you are all tightly blocked. The north gate is blocked, the south gate is blocked, the east gate is blocked, and the west gate is blocked; everything is blocked. It is difficult to follow when all directions are blocked. You are still in that state.

You need to clearly understand your own position. In other words, you need to understand your relationships clearly. You must know what kind of father’s son you are and have a firm belief that no one can deny that relationship. To do that, you need to undergo a lot of training.

There are new people here, right? I guess a mix of people has gathered. Even if you peel off your shell and marinate like fish in soy sauce and salt and grill it, you must have the capacity to do so. Only then can you do great things in the future. That way, even if you meet a mix of people, you won’t feel bad. To not feel bad while going with you, I must not leave you as you are. I must thoroughly examine, flip over, squeeze, peel, poke, and rub you to transform you. Is that okay? "Yes."

Oh, what are you talking about? You might think I want to eat you, but even if I do, I will eat you. I have gone to the mountains of Gangwon-do and cut the neck of a pig and sucked its blood. I have done the same with deer. I have practiced it all. If my will is fulfilled, what can’t I do?

You are following the teacher now, but many of you are just patchwork followers. Do you know what a patchwork follower is? It is someone who only needs you when they have leftovers. Is it right for a man to be born and die without doing anything? But you are all patchwork followers. That is why I am currently educating you for transformation.

Now, Japanese people are in a frenzy trying to meet someone from South Korea. However, I told them, "If you want to meet me, come with the same ideology as mine. Until then, I won’t meet you." I said I would handle it with strength without meeting them. I am still conducting such operations.

As young people in the university, do not become a troublesome group that is difficult to deal with. You must become a group that cannot be ignored even while sitting still.

When I was in prison, I mobilized the spiritual world without speaking and subdued my enemies. You must also lay the foundation of strength that can thoroughly subdue your enemies. If you do not have the belief that evil must succumb to good and cannot present the issues of your environment, you cannot become a central being in that environment. Because of these principles, you must know your own limits well.

When looking at the fortune of heaven and earth, there will come a time in the process of restoration where America cannot handle it on its own. That is why I prayed in front of the White House. I thought I would not end as a wanderer in South Korea but would establish some other foothold and leave.

To do that, many agents are needed. We need agents who can say it’s okay even if they are slapped on the back, hit on the cheek, or stepped on the head. Do you like that? "Yes." Do the ladies like it too? Is that still okay? "Yes." Where are you from? You came from Jeolla-do, right? "Yes." Earlier, there was a tall person over there; how would it feel if a tall person dated a small girl? (Laughter) In any case, there is no end to this kind of story. We haven’t even finished Act 1 yet. (Laughter) But let’s conclude here. Everyone, is it boring? Is it boring? "It’s not boring." It’s not boring? "Yes." Then that’s good. "I’m satisfied." I feel that my coming here was worthwhile.

Let us be mobilized as warriors for the establishment of a new culture. Today, the teacher woke up at 3:30 AM, washed his face, and started the day. These days, when I look at the river in Cheongpyeong, the weather suddenly gets cold, and steam rises from the river, which is very beautiful. I sat by the river and fished like a fisherman waiting for the passage of time. I am not fishing to catch carp. I am spending money that could buy hundreds of fish. Some of you might think, "We are starving; why not share that cost with us?" If you ask, I will give it to you. Why do I do this? Because by fishing, I can concentrate my mind.

Then, I hurriedly arrived in Sutak-ri, and it was 10:40. What time did you arrive? The teacher said he would come in the afternoon, but you came too early and wandered around Sutak-ri, urging, "Let it be noon, let it be noon." So, I left Sutak-ri five minutes before noon. If you say you will come in the afternoon but come in the morning, it feels bad. The teacher could say, "Oh, you said you would come at three in the afternoon, but you are already here?"

So, the teacher left Sutak-ri five minutes early and quietly prayed in the car since noon was prayer time.

What did the teacher first say? He said that Korea is not inferior to any country in the world. Therefore, university students should have the belief that Korea is not bad, carry the good nature of our country on their backs, embrace our national identity in their hearts, and create a new history with the ideology of a new world. That is what should be done in universities. Do you understand? "Yes."

If you do that, the decadent schools in America will not be a problem. No young people from any country will be a problem. We should start here with a new outfit, a new attitude, and a new belief to build a new tomorrow.

Historically, in terms of the environment of the times, and in terms of the heavenly fortune, we are not inferior to any ethnic group or nation. You must not defend your current position but break through it and expand your limits, crossing the boundaries of the university and society. You must cultivate the driving force that can cross Japan and the Pacific Ocean to the highest boundary of Western culture. To cross the heat, you need more than heat. To establish and manage a cultural world beyond the current culture, you need a driving force greater than that.

Therefore, you should start with the attitude of a man or woman with a hopeful heart, as warriors for the creation of a new culture. Do you understand? "Yes."

To do that, I must mobilize you now. So, raise your hand if you are willing to be mobilized. Good. Act 1 ends here. Speaking is this difficult. It is this hard to explain the principles. (The recording is not available after this point.)
October 4, 1969 (Saturday), Jeon Headquarters Church.

It could not be helped.  
So, what is salvation? In a word, it is returning to our original state. Then, there must be a standard for returning to the original state; what could that standard be?
