When He came, He came with the hope of finding the son of hope, but when He leaves, He does so with immense disappointment. How can we describe that, and how can we comfort Him?  
Father, we know that you are looking upon this poor Korean people with compassion. Until now, no one knew, but now we understand that behind the tears and blood of our people, the Father has been present throughout this miserable historical process.  
Now, as we reflect on history, we realize that the miserable history of this nation symbolizes the Father’s misery, and that the invasion faced by this nation surrounded by the world’s great powers resembles the Father’s lonely situation.  
We understand that there was a nation the Father lamented over and sought after, and that this was to bless someone connected to that nation. We stand in the unfortunate position of being able to charge forward centered on the heart of the Father, intertwined with the history of the Republic of Korea. However, now we realize that this is a great fortune, and we cannot help but thank the Father.  
This nation has not been able to find the path it should take since liberation. The Christianity that represented this nation has failed to take responsibility, and this nation remains an unnamed country that has yet to join the UN. Therefore, Father, please bring an end to this nation’s suffering.  
We must understand that we are both the children of the Father and His envoys who have received the solemn heavenly mission to ensure that the nations of the world bow their heads to this nation.  
Father, I have come to realize that I was born with a destiny that I cannot abandon this nation, even if I die, throughout my 50 years of life. So even in the path of rejection, in sorrow, loneliness, and injustice, I have rather held onto and comforted the Father. I thank you for allowing me to have such time.  
If I had not known the Father’s heart, I realize I could not stand as a subject left in history. Although the sorrows of history may have passed, the heart intertwined with the Father remains, becoming my treasure and an unassailable condition. I understand that all of this was not a cunning plan to ruin me, but a loving favor for me.  
Now, I will not dream of peace in my future life. I have no desire to seek pleasure while singing songs of happiness. Thus, I am still struggling to maintain the appearance of a brave person who can sing the song of great victory representing the world and the universe as your son.  
Even if I do not seek you, I know you want to love me. You know that I am struggling not to leave any opposing conditions before your heart. On any day, whether awake or asleep, every aspect of my life and every thought is filled with the single-minded intention of serving you. I know this is a record of merit before the Father and a treasure, so all must inherit this holy heart of victory.  
We, who have been born from the bloodline of those who incited the building of the history of resentment and the walls of sorrow before the Father, are here, but the young people gathered here know the Father’s sorrowful circumstances. Therefore, may they come to understand that no matter how high the walls built are, they have a destiny to overcome them. Even if there is a river that serves as a boundary, may they realize that they must connect ropes and build bridges to cross.  
Before the solemn command of heaven, even if I blame my shortcomings and try to offer them to the Father, I realize that the time has not yet been granted. However, I know that there are those who are striving day and night, even in dreams, to find that day when they can offer all of themselves, even in their shortcomings, before you. History has unfolded in this way, so I earnestly hope and wish that the young men and women gathered here can become those who can do so in this reality.  
The one who felt sorrow, injustice, unhappiness, and pain in the past was the Father, and I have come to understand that only the son who pioneered this path has experienced this. Therefore, in the reality where there are tasks remaining to mature this historical work, I earnestly wish that even one more person can be added here, who can praise this achievement and inherit it, so that they can be a group that the Father can be proud of.  
These are your children from the universities gathered from all over the country. What path are they on? The university, which must take responsibility for the future of the Republic of Korea, is in a state of confusion. However, now is the time to present a charge and plant the flag of victory, so I earnestly hope and wish that we can be the heavenly princes and princesses who have received the Father’s mission to fulfill our responsibilities.  
When we came here, we were merely young people flowing aimlessly, but now we must leave with a burden that no one can shift. We must carry the dark clouds of sorrow with us.  
We have learned through history that it is difficult to establish a connection of unity without passing through the altar of blood as a sacrifice to overcome the resentment of the nation. We have also learned that we must do so in our time today. Therefore, in this time when that mission is being urged every moment, I earnestly hope and wish that the young people gathered here can become those who can rise up with torches, complying with the Father, to fulfill their responsibility to lay down their blood and flesh for this nation, in every corner of this country.  
The brothers of the world are following us. If we do not take responsibility, they will cry out that they will take on the burden instead, but please do not allow us to pass on the difficult baton of the cross to them. I earnestly hope that by fulfilling our responsibilities, we can prepare a foundation for the altar that will please the Father, equipping ourselves with the authority of the elder brother. After that, may they bow their heads before the Father and worship and praise with tears of gratitude, leaving such feelings in the hearts of your young people.  
This is something that must be crossed in our time, and this is the mission of the young people of this era. Please allow us to exert all our strength for this responsibility. I earnestly ask and wish that we may become the heavenly sons and daughters who can rise up with clenched fists to build a new morning of light.  
The remaining days are calling us, and we know that this poor nation is calling us. Please allow your children, who are putting forth all their efforts to fulfill that responsibility even in the environment of learning, to be those who can live not just for today, but for tomorrow.  
Please do not let us become cowards before the hope of tomorrow, but allow us to be strong and courageous heavenly warriors. I earnestly ask that your children may leave behind victories before the world and pass on victories to the future.  
Now, please allow us to have strong and courageous hearts, and when we collide with a rock, let the rock break, and when we collide with steel, let the steel break, so that we may swear to dedicate our entire lives before the Father, and let us return with that conviction.  
May we be your children who can receive the Father’s assurance in tomorrow’s heaven, and may we be your children who can receive your praise. I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

The Turning Point of Good and Evil  
<Prayer> Father, please carefully lead those who are responsible for resolving the historical resentment while becoming the offering of victory left for future generations.  
We must not become those who betray you or turn back upon seeing you on this perilous path. Also, please do not allow these individuals to become fallen ones who wish to bear the heavy burdens they carry but cannot.  
Since we are walking the path with a cross proportional to our circumstances and positions, please allow us to become your children who can resonate with the deep heart of the Father and digest the heart of the heavenly world.  
Now we have passed through September 1969 and welcomed October. October has been a month of joy in the historical process and a month in which we have returned joy and glory to the Father with the dawn of a new day. Therefore, Father, please allow this month to be one in which all our steps can be in harmony with your will.  
Though we may appear anxious as we gather in your sanctuary, we must become a group that can gather our hearts and command. The Father, who has been buried in deep heart for 6,000 years, has revealed that since I have come this way, I must go this way, and on the morning of October 5, 1969, I must overcome the enemy and secure the glory of victory. Therefore, we must become a group that can command the path of destiny for ourselves. Father, holding your beloved sons and daughters, we must recall all the resentments of human history and become children who can praise you and deepen our connection with you.  
Today, we recognize that all the emotions we feel and everything we possess are not connected to you, Father. While we have received grace through the connection of creation, we also know that all the environments, nations, and world we exist in today did not begin with you, but with the enemy, Satan. The emotions we feel do not arise from the connection with the Father but from the shadow of death, and they manifest in a realm where the enemy can rejoice. Therefore, we must not hesitate in this fight today. We must not forget that we must fight to overcome these emotions tomorrow.  
It is not easy to subdue a nation or the world, but we have come to understand how difficult it is to subdue our own insignificant emotions to become the origin of heaven, to embody your heart, and to eliminate all sources of the enemy. We must overcome this peak. We must overcome it before we die. We must overcome it before the dawn of the new year.  
Thus, when I can embrace the Father, whom I miss and long for, and call out to him without shame, I hope for the day when I can say, "You are my Father, and I am your son," in a place where there is no gap or third party. I wish to be a son who can recognize himself as one who is connected to the Father’s source and heart, and who is for the Father.  
May we become sons who can say that through you, the Father has forgotten the resentment of history, that through you, a connection of history will be established, and that a new origin of history will be established through you. May we, centered on the Father, welcome the day of fulfillment of wishes, charging forward with vigor towards families, tribes, nations, and the world, praising the glory of the Father and aspiring to be part of the glorious ranks of victory. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.
This morning, your children scattered across the world are infinitely longing for the Korean land in this faraway Asia. They are praying and admiring as they hope for the day to come to this land, staying up all night. Your children are spread across the globe. The cross they bear is a substitute for your cross, and the battlefields they go to are on your behalf. Even if they are far away, please allow them to be your children embraced in your arms, and do not let them stray from the bond of family.

The more we understand your holiness, the more we realize that behind that holiness lies much sorrow and many stories. We must melt those things with tears and with the sweat and blood of our efforts. Although there is a historical and tragic story of having to challenge new aspects while shedding tears and blood, please have compassion on those who are determined to walk the path of tears and blood.

Even if we bear the cross of tears you left behind, whether we take the shortcut or the long way around, Father, please do not let us forget our loyalty and integrity towards you. In leaving behind the integrity and loyalty of your sons and daughters that you desire on this earth, please do not let us lose the bonds of family and kinship.

Since you have worked hard to come to us, please help these children to be equipped with the justification of being your children, and do not let them tarnish your dignity even if they die. I earnestly hope and wish that they do not become those who diminish your face and authority, Father.

The foreign family members are missing this place in Korea dearly as October arrives. They are focusing their devotion on the holy places chosen in 40 countries around the world, and I know they are preparing to be dispatched again this year.

Father, every time we hear news from all over the world, we think about how much you long to hear the news that your will will spread across this Korean land one day, and how much you desire to see your sons spreading out in all directions towards the enemy. Therefore, Father, please protect their paths, and let them go forth with strength, courage, and boldness to break down the final barriers and establish the lighthouse of victory. Let them be a group that can break down the walls of the enemy and build the eternal and unchanging kingdom of yours.

Today, your children are gathered everywhere to worship you, and I earnestly hope that you will be with them. Your children, who will be connected in the future, know many things on this earth, so please be with those who are devoting themselves.

I earnestly ask and wish that you mobilize all ancestors to guide those who are infinitely thirsty and wandering towards heaven to become indispensable offerings that dedicate themselves to building a heavenly nation and a heavenly people as a unified group.

At this time, please remember the children gathered here. I earnestly hope and wish that you will be with the young people who are pioneering in various places.

I have conveyed all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words>
The turning point of good and evil (writing on the board) is a sad situation for us humans to be in a position to speak of this turning point of good and evil. However, not only individuals but also families, tribes, nations, and the world are at this turning point of good and evil, and the historical process that has flowed until now is about how to resolve this fate. Moreover, even countless people struggling on the path of faith in the name of religion have not been able to cross the boundary of this turning point and continue to fight.

Humans must eliminate the turning point that remains before God. Even when looking at individuals, we must recognize that we are at this turning point of good and evil. If an individual crosses this turning point, there is a turning point that the family must cross. Even if the family has crossed this turning point, the nation must also surpass that standard. Even if the nation has surpassed that standard, the world must also go beyond that standard.

Furthermore, when looking at God, there remains a turning point that cannot be crossed due to human fallibility. We must understand that this turning point exists. Today, the turning point that fallen humanity must cross is an inevitable limit that must be crossed by fallen humanity, and God must also cross this turning point. However, from God's perspective, this is a turning point that should not exist, with no connection or relationship.

So how will God cross this turning point? God is omnipotent, so it should not be a problem, but it becomes an issue because He cannot cross it alone. The center of this problem is not God but us humans. Not only is the entire humanity blocked at this turning point, but every individual that makes up the world is in this turning point as a consequence of the fall, and we must recognize that God is also unable to cross this turning point.

When we think of the place of happiness and ideals that God longs for, can the turning point of good and evil disappear in the history of humanity today? This does not only refer to the disappearance for some individuals or some nations but asks whether it can disappear before the entire world. To do so, the world must cross to a position where it can align with God, who should not have a turning point of good and evil. Otherwise, we must understand that a turning point remains before God.

When we look at the mission of restoration today, the right side pursues good while the left side pursues evil. Good is pulling me from the front, while evil is pulling me from behind. Above, God is trying to protect me, while below, Satan is trying to bring me down. However, this evil has dominated more than half of history. Not only half.

Humanity has suffered from endless struggles between good and evil. Today, we know that most of the fallen history has started with evil and has brought about evil results. When we look at our individual lives living in such a history, from the moment we greet the morning until we go to bed at night, our daily lives are spent in the struggle of how to sustain our own bodies amidst the fight between good and evil.

In our daily lives, most of the time is not spent in good but rather in evil. This shows that evil is close to us and aligns with our current environment. In such circumstances, finding the authority of good that allows us to go in the direction we wish without being hindered by the evil environment is an extremely difficult issue. We know through the Bible that Paul also struggled with this situation.

Oh, wretched man that I am! Who will deliver me from this body of death? (Romans 7:24) He expressed that the path of carrying his cross is not smooth. Considering this fact, we can see that not only Paul but also many saints and sages throughout history have not been able to resolve the issue of wretchedness in their lives.

We understand that the limits that must be overcome through such difficult trials and tribulations have remained too tedious in the life paths of countless people who have gone through historical eras. Such tedious paths have not only been blocked in historical times but have continued to this day, standing before the respected positions you hold or the life paths you cherish. Thus, standing before the path of fate that we cannot avoid with our eyes open, evil remains and occupies the entire area. Therefore, how to establish the subjective authority that can clear such boundaries is a historical concern, a contemporary concern, and the most important issue in pursuing our real lives.

When we step over this limit of concern and welcome the victorious morning where we can raise our hands in joy and praise good, singing with the rays of the bright sun, and when we can praise the joy of a day and go to bed with smiles, we must recognize that it is not a simple matter to become a qualified person who can fully digest a day of life.

We must resolve to eliminate evil from our own selves and environments. If we could live as we please, we would take that path without hesitation, but our fate as the children of misfortune does not allow us to do so, and we can only sigh.

We must make a new commitment to prevent evil in our lives. The question of when we will take responsibility to draw our swords and cut away the evil in this environment is a pressing issue before us at this turning point. Here, the question arises of when we will exert our strength to eliminate evil from this environment. Without a time to remove evil from our surroundings, the lines of death that weave a miserable fate in our life paths will surround us, and we will have no way to cross this unfortunate limit.

If we can deny the demands of our own bodies and move towards an unchanging, shining appearance with a single purpose, we must recognize how precious that time is. To have such a day, we must be able to transform all the sorrow and all the elements of resentment and evil that have arisen from the failures to evil throughout history into elements of joy in good. You must become a master in that transformation. Otherwise, we will not be able to prepare a point where God can be present even for a single day.

If we cannot conclude the life concept of yesterday and today, no matter how excellent the seed we have, that seed cannot bear good fruit. Therefore, when making a new resolution, we must resolve to restore and compensate for everything that has been resolved in the historical era and confront it proportionally, aiming to leave something behind. This attitude is extremely important in our lives that must cross the turning point of good and evil.

Do not lose your first heart towards God. When you recognize that your heart pursues good and truth, and you forget everything until now and lean towards a single purpose, and when your entire life is governed by those things, that moment is the starting point where good can relate to you. When such a moment occurs, you must resolve to sacrifice everything and pledge all your integrity to protect and pioneer that moment. If you do not become someone who can deeply feel and cherish the sorrow in such a position, you will not be able to establish the point of good in navigating today's environment and in the tedious journey.

If you cannot connect such a heart to the next day, you will have to fight again. Therefore, if there is a condition of good that has been established, you must become someone who makes every effort to not lose that condition. If the heart of loving God has surged up in your faith journey, that first heart! That first heart! That first heart is something that cannot be exchanged for a fortune. If you lose that first heart, you cannot re-establish a loving relationship with God.

If you have a fervent heart towards God and have resolved to become His child, that is the most precious time. Therefore, you must not become someone who sells that time cheaply.

God comes out seeking truth. He has brought truth worth ten thousand and has promised to give truth worth ten thousand, so we must bring the results of that truth. However, if we humans cannot bring the results of that truth, God will turn away with a sad step. This is not due to God but due to ourselves.

When such a time comes, we must be prepared to protect it even at the cost of our lives. The promise and connection of that time will surely come to me, and to meet that day, I must quietly prepare myself, expanding the foundation of my nature centered on myself, waiting for that moment without asking anyone.

When we trace the path of humanity or the path of history, many people have pursued victory after victory, but there has never been a victory recognized by heaven and earth or a victory that can be said to be our true nature.

So when will that hour come? We must wait and yearn for that time more earnestly than anyone preparing for any battle, more earnestly than any nation preparing for war, and more earnestly than any individual preparing to achieve a single purpose. And when the time comes, we must seize it completely.

Therefore, when we see good people or good deeds, it is because our wishes are being fulfilled in the environment, so we must forget ourselves and have a heart that can fully graft ourselves to that and completely submit to that work. Even if we deny ourselves a thousand or ten thousand times, if there is a true standard, a true appearance, and a true essence, we must fully align ourselves with it. This attitude of life is absolutely necessary for us, who are placing the boundary of evil before us today.

Have you ever had a time in your faith life that you cannot forget? If not, you must have such a time someday. If there is a day when you cannot contain the heart of longing and admiration for God that explodes deep within you, a day when you struggle because of it, know that a blessing more precious than any fortune on this earth is planted and connected there.

To find such a day, history has surged forth, and countless people have shed blood in suffering on the crossroads of history. Therefore, when that day comes, we must stand in a position to take on the turning point of our ancestors' sorrowful history, gathering the devotion that replaces a thousand years of history. With that, along with the rising longing towards heaven, when we have the heart to melt away all the roots of historical sins hidden in our bones and shed tears, God will be with us, the kingdom of heaven will be with us, and the people of heaven will also be with us.

Jesus Christ, who took on the shame of humanity. We must understand that God has been searching for such individuals and families, and such tribes, nations, and countries throughout the hearts of humanity until now.

When we think about this, it raises the question of whether thirty million people can have such a heart to seek heaven, and whether such a nation can exist on this earth. God desires that not a single person be excluded, that all citizens have a heart longing for heaven, saying, "This is the homeland of good, so come quickly, God, who comes as the essence of good."
how much have you longed for a country that can be? We must think about how great God's efforts must be in seeking such a country on earth. 

When you plant beans, you get beans; when you plant red beans, you get red beans. This is an inevitable fact in the causal relationships of the natural world. However, we know that despite having the inherent desire to pursue truth, the true essence of that nature has not yet manifested. We must hold onto the fact that we were born as beings contrary to our original mind and walk the path of life. We were not born as true human beings with our nature sown in us, but rather as distorted and deformed human forms.

If I claim to know the inherent duty of humanity, which should be pursued and lived according to divine relationships, then I am a shameful being who cannot present myself before the true posture and character of my original self. Yet, looking at the countless humans throughout history who have raised their heads and acted without knowing their shame, as well as those living in the world today, we must see the humanity of this world that does not recognize its own shame and consider it my own shame, striving to cover it up, and there must be someone who is concerned about hiding that flaw. But if there is not even one person who can do that, can there be hope in the world?

From this perspective, Jesus Christ came as such a being in the course of human history. Humanity is in a position where it cannot escape the greatest final judgment punishment, greater than any prisoner of historical times, without knowing the shame of being naked. They are in a position where they cannot forget their shame. Nevertheless, there must be one who should be on this earth, who takes the shame of humanity, which has forgotten such shame, as his own and covers it up, and that person is Jesus Christ, who came as the parent of humanity.

So what did He do on this earth? He took on the responsibility of tracing the misery of humanity deeply hidden in the hearts of humanity, rooted in their marrow, to unearth the source of good and eliminate the source of evil. Without doing so, no matter how much we think and cover up, it cannot reach humanity, and no matter how much effort is made, without breaking through all boundaries globally, it cannot establish a relationship between humanity and the parent. You must understand that Jesus Christ lived within such relational rights and fought until he died.

Living in such a position, how tragic it is that we, who do not know the shame of being in such a position, demand happiness and seek to find our own tasks among us! How pitiful it is! How often must God, who is in a subjective position that should start and decide everything with only good in mind, have wanted to blow up this sinful world all at once? It must have been more than ten million times.

Good cannot be established without a loving relationship with God.

Individuals have betrayed as individuals, families have betrayed as families, and nations have betrayed as nations. In the midst of such history, what should we, who have taken up the banner of unification today, do? We must fundamentally eliminate such things.

If we have one wish, what is it? It is that we must think about God more than anyone else, more than any saint or wise person who has thought about God throughout history. We must concentrate all our senses and perceptions centered on the comprehensive sensory cells of our nervous system, to love heaven supremely at any time and in any environment, without yielding for even a moment, and to start from heaven, live for heaven, and return to heaven. In other words, we must start from good, live in good, and return to good. It is not an easy task to think from this perspective.

God, standing in the position of a parent, feels a loving stimulus toward His children, and that is good. There is no doubt that there was an emotion that arose from His original mind, which could not help but love centered on Adam and Eve. When He looked at all things and saw that they were good, we can understand that good cannot be established without a loving relationship with God.

Because humans have the origin that God boasts of as His beloved sons and daughters, as long as a standard that can forget that origin does not exist, humans can remain as objects of longing and demand before God. However, those who do not feel this must understand that it is harder for humanity to go to God's love than for God to come to humanity with a heart of love. This is because there is no model.

You must understand that you are in such a position.

Because of this position, God looks upon humanity with compassion and pity. Because humanity is in such a position, God can look upon humanity with pity. Yet, if humanity, even in that position, has the appearance of respecting and loving God, even in a figurative sense, and has a relative form in the direction that God seeks, how pleased God would be!

A newborn baby does not know the parents who look at its face. However, after about three months, the baby will smile back at the welcoming face of its mother. The baby does not know that it is its mother, nor does it know the love of its mother, but the mother feels the greatest joy from the baby's smile, which responds to her in a relative position. This is because the love of the parents pours out through the emotional connection that is linked beyond the value of the whole.

In the same way, God has the standard of experience that can be said to love us, but humanity does not have the standard of experience that can be said to love God. Through relationships, we can be in the position of sons and daughters before God, so we can call God our Father. How wonderful it would be if we could be in such a relationship, even if we do not know why we should call Him Father! However, humanity has fallen from the position where it cannot think of God, who has a love relationship that pierces to the bone. If these humans, whose hearts are closed to God, even have a relative form before such a God, God will pour out all the love that is hidden in His heart upon them.

Moreover, when you come to know heaven and start on the path to heaven, just like a child, God will pour out all grace and love upon you. He will make you feel that you are the most important. 

In heaven and on earth, I am the most important. He will lift you up to that point. So, how far does He want to raise you? Even though you know nothing, you will center on the idea that you are the most important. He will advise you that you have been chosen to represent your nation. There is no one else like you in the world. Then, you will suddenly think, "Ah, God is making me this way and has made this promise." Most people think that way. But no, you must understand that this is a call to establish a love relationship that can lead to that.

If there is a promise, does that promise just come true? No, it does not. You must bring all the love relationships that can correspond to that promise and align them with good, to create the origin that can unify and determine the content of the subject. In other words, you must strive to establish a love relationship. Yet, despite this, most people have fallen away while pursuing only the promise itself without establishing that love relationship.

It is foolish for a child to act and behave based on the standard of being told by their parents that they are good. Being told they are good is merely a means to bring them closer to the loving heart that the parents desire.

The great discovery made possible by the Unification Church

When we look at the fall centered on the turning point of good and evil in our emotional world, we see that the stages of rebirth, growth, and perfection, which are two-thirds of the way, remain within the realm of the fall. Then, is the one-third stage of perfection a standard of hope that humanity can pursue? This is something we have not yet experienced in the course of human history. Therefore, it is buried. It is buried within your original nature. At times, it may shake and stir at the very bottom of your heart, but it is exceedingly difficult to establish a heart world that can connect with God beyond the standards of the heavenly world.

What has the Unification Church presented to the world today? It has not given you money, nor has it brought you social success. It has presented the conditions of goodness that dwell within your original nature, that is, the center of goodness that can establish a relationship with God. It has not presented anything else.

It is a remarkable thing that a person who could not love God can now love God, and a person who only knew their parents can now know someone greater than their parents and praise that person's love. If someone who could not know love beyond the love between a husband and wife has now experienced love beyond that, it is undoubtedly a great discovery and a great experience. If someone who only knew their own children can now think of the people of the world as their own children and act accordingly, that is also a great discovery. This great discovery has been made possible by the Unification Church today.

The issue is that this has been made possible by the Unification Church. This is not something that has been achieved within the historical limits. Until now, the love relationships have been limited to couples, families, societies, and nations within the realm of the fall. There has been no one in this world who could rise above that. If love relationships could have been established that love beyond parents, love beyond couples, and love beyond children, such problems would not have arisen. However, such love relationships have never been established. When we establish a new worldview, a new national view, a new family view, and a new lifestyle based on the absence of such content and the absence of such static standards, it will become the origin that presents a new boundary in this evil world.

To eradicate this evil world, there must be some origin, right? This is not an origin of money, nor an origin of power, nor an origin of any glory of the world. That origin must not be an external origin that is pursued relatively, but must be established from within itself. It must be something that existed before I was here and that I had before I was born. What could that be? That is God's love.

Only love is the foundation of eternal life and the fulfillment of purpose.

God created the heavens and the earth to feel joy. What is joy? It is goodness. To be good, things must go as one wishes. So, what is the highest thing that can go as one wishes? When you seek the peak of that, there is nothing but love.

Why did He create all things? He created them to be joyful. Then, what is the thing that brings the greatest joy? It is neither money nor power. The greatest joy for an orphan is the resurrection of their parents. For a virtuous woman whose husband has died, the greatest joy is the resurrection of her husband. For parents who have lost their children, the greatest joy is the resurrection of their deceased child. Why? Because a foundation is needed to overcome death. A love relationship that is established through resurrection by breaking through the barrier of death is necessary. For an orphan who has lost their parents, having a parental relationship that can empathize with their position is the greatest joy. Love All People
I understand that you have gathered here representing the members who are worshiping nationwide, so I will speak briefly.

The Root of Existence and the Connection of Providence
As you can see, it is now autumn. In autumn, one feels a desolate mood. We have passed through spring and summer and are just before winter.

The beauty of nature changes with the seasons. If we take trees as an example, the leaves change with the seasons. However, the branches and trunk do not change. When autumn comes, the leaves fall, but it is because those leaves were there that the branches and trunk grew. This is just an example of trees, but the principle applies to a nation as well.

Even when centered on a nation, the same principle applies. When we consider the Republic of Korea, it has sprouted from roots, formed a trunk, and extended branches. The countless people who have been born and lived in the Republic of Korea, or who have already passed away, are like leaves. Therefore, even if the leaves fall, the trunk and branches of the Republic of Korea continue to develop.

The same goes for God's will. When we consider the entire providence, it is the same. With God as the root, through religion as the trunk, countless believers have gone through the journey of life. Those who have passed through have contributed to the growth of the providential road, just as branches and trunks grow.

There are four seasons: spring, summer, autumn, and winter. Winter will come soon, but this shows that nature cannot exist outside of a certain relationship. Similarly, humans cannot exist outside of some connection. For a person to be born, there must be parents like roots. And there are siblings born from those parents. Siblings are like branches. Through these siblings, parents can gain glory or misfortune. Thus, you must understand that any existence arises through connections like roots.

When it comes to siblings, there can be both males and females. They are like branches sprouting from one trunk. Just as there are main branches and side branches, there are also main siblings and side siblings.

Because siblings are bound by an unbreakable connection, they must be valued. That connection is not one that they have made themselves; it is a connection made through their parents.

Therefore, that connection cannot be altered by them. It cannot be manipulated according to their whims. Because they are siblings bound by such connections, they must respect that connection. Thus, no matter how bad the relationship between siblings may be, they cannot escape this connection because they are related to one root.

The same is true when looking at nations. There are many sovereigns in numerous countries, but those sovereigns are also bound by some historical flow.

They are connected not only to the history of their own country but also to the flow of the world. Moreover, if there is an absolute being, all nations are formed around the connection with that being. Therefore, based on the historical direction in which the world flows, each nation is bound by an inseparable connection. That connection cannot be blocked by the power of the state. Because they follow that connection, all nations cannot escape from it.

When we look at this in relation to our members today, you gathered here as individuals, but there was some connection that allowed you to gather. That connection is not something you created. It is a providential connection. Because there was a connection that made it impossible not to gather, you are here today. Because of that connection, relationships have been formed, and we cannot live outside of this position.

When we look at a family, the husband and wife did not meet by chance. They have come together through countless historical processes, weaving together many life paths.

If we delve into that connection, we find the history of the Republic of Korea and the history of the world. Further, we find that God's providential history is embedded within it.

Respect the Connections and Relationships Between Humans
Through these vast and wide connections, relationships have been formed among us humans. This is true not only for humans but also for all of nature.

When we think of these relationships, we cannot simply regard the parents who allowed your individual existence lightly. When we consider the connection with parents, it is akin to representing and synthesizing heaven and earth.

When we say that there are 3.6 billion people in the world, we can say there are 1.8 billion men and 1.8 billion women, and parents have formed relationships representing those 1.8 billion men and women. The representative figures in the position where all male and female relationships are collectively summarized are the parents who have established a relationship with you. And because we are born centered on such parents, when we look at the world’s 3.6 billion people, we see that all humanity is, in that sense, the same siblings.

In a broader sense, this is how humanity can manifest as a collective entity. This means that humanity was created by God, and thus can connect to God's relationships.

Why do I say this? Because today we see a tendency to neglect human relationships. It is easy to end with just a greeting when we meet in the morning. Even when dealing with neighbors, it should not end with merely recognizing them as someone we see every day or as the father of someone we know. If we look more meaningfully, human relationships carry great significance, yet we do not regard them as important. That is why I am saying this.

When you deal with an individual, if that person gives you a bad impression or has caused you harm at some point, you may feel displeased. You may even consider them an enemy and seek revenge.

However, if you delve deeper into the connection with that person, you will find that there is a greater connection than the current enmity. That connection possesses a higher and deeper value than the enmity established at present. Even with such a connection, if you treat them as an enemy, not only will nothing be resolved, but you may find yourself in a position to be criticized instead. Such complex and intricate relationships exist among humans.

That is why we, or those who practice the way, say to perform good deeds and to reconcile with enemies. They say this because behind every individual, there are connections, and everything that appears within the historical realm is related. There are connections that are more valuable and noble than the standards by which one feels and criticizes. Therefore, if you mishandle that, you may find yourself in a position to be criticized by your own self.

Thus, when dealing with people, you must put in effort and cherish the relationships with those you interact with.

Where People Who Love Each Other Live is Heaven
So, when we look at humans, how can we establish the highest connections of love? And when we consider those with whom we have formed connections, where is the highest place to love them? First, we must think of heaven, then the earth, and then of people. However, thinking of heaven and earth is too vague. For example, when we think of the earth, it is unclear what we should think about the earth.

So, what is the concrete and substantial center? It is humans. Therefore, we must love humans with a heart that loves heaven and a heart that loves the earth. Loving humans is how we establish the highest connections among relationships.

When it comes to the world of virtue, what kind of person can be called a person of character? The standard for that is whether or not they can love people in the true sense.

So why do we like God? It is not because God asks us to love Him. It is because God loves humanity. When someone loves humanity, that person represents humanity and loves God. And because God loves humanity, we come to love Him. Ultimately, the secret to becoming a child of God and drawing closer to God is to become someone who can love people more than anyone else. When viewed through the lens of relationships, such a person can be placed in the highest position.

When we look at the principles of our Unification Church and the Book of Genesis, we can see that all creation was made for the sake of humanity. Moreover, the ideal world we desire also exists for humanity.

That is why a world that loves love and knows how to care for people is heaven. Heaven is not something separate. The world where people who care for and love others live is heaven. Happiness is not something separate either.

So, where is that place where people care for and love others? When we look at ourselves today, the place where we can love people and elevate ourselves is the family. When parents look at their children, even if that child is a foolish little rascal with nothing to boast about, parents love that child more than anyone else. The family is a place filled with love and a place where one can elevate oneself. It is a place where one can manifest oneself with infinite value. That is the happy place.

We yearn for the kingdom of God. Why is that? Because it is a place where love exists. It is not temporary love, but a place where eternal love can endure beyond time. It is also a place where one can receive elevation and have their value recognized one hundred percent. In other words, it is a place of eternal happiness. That is why humans long for and yearn for the kingdom of heaven.

is to form a society where God can participate and to establish a nation. That is why we were born today.

Even when looking at the connections centered around an individual today, we can categorize them as either indirect or direct. There is also a difference in loving people, whether it is direct or indirect. However, they cannot be separated from each other. 

Loving a fellow citizen as a person of the Republic of Korea is a direct love, while loving a foreigner is an indirect love. Just because it is indirect does not mean we can separate it from the direct perspective. They are not unrelated; there is definitely a connection.

If I meet once, I have to meet twice, and if I have lunch with them, I have to have dinner with them, and then I will have to become friends and colleagues. Even if we become friends, there is a world of difference between my friendship and their friendship. I know that if we meet, we will inevitably part ways within a few meetings, and there are many conditions that cannot be combined, so I do not engage in such matters. However, I do take the initiative to share and give. 

The same goes for Japan. We have cast our operational net across Japan, moving young people as we please. This has become a significant issue in Japan. So in the future, certain influential figures in Japan will come to Cheongpyeong, wanting to see the teacher, and even if they ask not to report it in the news, they will end up following to report it. Such times will come in the not-so-distant future. 

You may not know it well because you are all family. A family member does not know if their father is great. The son of a president does not call his father "President" but "Dad." The dad who eats is the same now as he was in the past; he has not changed in any significant way. So, the thought of going abroad representing 30 million people with the title of president is something they would never dream of. When they are in their father's arms, they are just happy because he is their dad. That is why they do not know. You also think of the teacher as just a father, so you do not know what I am like. 

Do not oppose the Unification Church lightly. If you are going to oppose it, then you should cut off the head of the Unification Church's Reverend Moon and oppose it. Do you understand what I mean?
As long as I am alive, there is nothing strange about opposing me no matter how much you do. I am that kind of person. Do not think lightly of it. When I speak with you, it means I know what kind of heart you have. I have lived my life facing the emotional worlds of many people. Just by blinking my eyes once, I can tell what that person is thinking. However, when I ask, "Are you thinking this way right now?" they say no. They think that way but deny it. Then I say, "Oh, you are thinking this way, so don’t think useless thoughts." This is a quick way to catch a person. If you do this a few times, the operation will succeed. The teacher has carried out such operations until now.

In my mind, there is only victory. Moderation or conventionalism will not do. We must tighten our belts and move forward. The young people here must have come today thinking, "Let’s go to church once." What brought you here? What are you here to do? Did you come to do business? Did you come to get something to eat? There must be a purpose. You must have the determination that you will become this kind of person, that you will definitely become this way. The teacher is a person who goes forward centered on this determination. However, you have none of this and just follow along, so you get tired after running a little. Now is the time to mobilize everything; can we just kick with our feet? Wouldn't it be nice if we could kick?

In my mind, there is only victory. So, is there a difference between older and younger people? In this case, older people become a hindrance. Therefore, this work should be centered on young people; since we cannot kill them, we must hit them to make them understand, even if it leaves bruises. Young people like it even if their bones are broken. To carry out this work, we have prevented ordinary people from being called in.

You are warriors of unification. When we say warriors, what kind of warrior is it? Is it the warrior of death (死) or the scholar (士)? The scholar is better than the warrior of death, right? Then is just sitting still being a scholar? A scholar is someone who turns the heavens and the earth upside down. Therefore, when I faced the German people, I thought, "You guys, it’s good to meet you. God has struggled for 6,000 years to meet you." The same thought occurred when I went to Japan. When I got off the plane at Haneda Airport in Japan, I thought the same thing. During the era of Japanese imperialism, did all the officials welcome the emperor when he returned?

The teacher wants to work centered on the people of our country more than any other country. Even when traveling, when I arrive, people say, "The teacher is coming! The teacher is coming!" and they wait among themselves, thinking that when I arrive, it must be a dream. Even when I travel around the world, I think of it as flying freely. Even though they know I am riding in a car, they think that way.

So, it is hard to match the rhythm there. The teacher saw this first during the second world tour. Foreign family members are champions in loyalty. How can I easily go before them, who have loyalty at the world's standards? That is the problem. Therefore, we must pray from the bottom. We must do it until the end; we must not get tired. We must pray until the end.

In the future, when we go abroad to speak, we must have interpreters. But there must be someone who wants to interpret. If no one wants to interpret, but we must interpret, what do we do? I have to speak and interpret myself, so what do I do? Therefore, I must go to Japan. I have lectured in Japanese on the podium in Japan after 21 years. When I speak Japanese, I do it much faster than the old Japanese people. I learned it in advance, thinking that there would come a time when I would use it.

Now I speak slowly, but if I speak quickly, my tongue hurts. At first, I spoke very slowly. However, when someone else speaks one word, I would be in a position to say ten words, but when someone else speaks one word, I couldn’t even say half a word. How could I lead people from another world? At first, when this peaceful person came to Seoul, I couldn’t keep up with how fast people spoke, no matter how fast I tried. But to match the pace of people’s conversations, I had to speak quickly too. There was a landlady who was short and spoke so fast that when she started talking early in the morning, it was overwhelming. Listening to her made me feel bad from the morning. By the time I asked for food, she had already eaten and digested it. It was very unpleasant. So, for six months, I went into a small room and practiced pronunciation from the basics, starting from the Korean alphabet. I trained until I grasped all the pronunciations. That’s how my speech got faster. My tone can also be corrected.

The mission of unification warriors. The teacher must convey vast teachings within a limited time, so I cannot speak with any dignity. If I do that, I won’t be able to say everything I need to say. Therefore, what the teacher says in one hour is equivalent to what others say in five hours. When it’s busy, I push forward. It means to be alert. Because of this, the front line of restoration has not been lost until now. Because of this, the teacher has not been lost and has brought forth the providence of restoration. Even if the Republic of Korea opposes and the whole world opposes, everything has been caught and overcome by the teacher. Just as the spirit world did, since there was opposition in Korea, we must fight to restore everything that has been opposed to the world’s standards. Therefore, we must unite all the family members abroad.

The teacher has gone through various processes. So, you should not just know the teacher as a shabby Unification Church teacher. The teacher is someone who weighs the times. Just like the fisherman who fished in the Yangtze River, he is someone who plays such games. In the future, there will come a time when you must bear a heavy mission. Therefore, to traverse all of Asia, you must have the determination to carry a bag and go to the Mongolian continent and the Siberian continent. The teacher has been carrying out such operations since birth. Even now, I am engaged in serious battles that you do not know about. You must know in which area of the front line of restoration you will carry out your mission. You must either become a communicator, an artilleryman, or an infantryman. You must become a group that can remain as historical figures in some area of the providential front line; this is the inevitable mission of unification warriors.

When we look at all the events occurring externally, there are many sorrowful times. If the Unification Church had not faced opposition, think about how much progress we would have made. If only a few people had listened to the teacher without opposition, today the Unification Church would have become a global church, and the destiny of heaven would have progressed along with the destiny of the Unification Church. You must take the lead in front of the nation and people. You must also take the lead in patriotism and love for your nation. As the leaders of internal missions, as the Abel-type leaders, you must understand that you are responsible for the overall mission before the nation.

The foundations we are building. In bringing the Unification Church this far, I have crossed countless hills. While crossing those hills, where did I meet you? At the hilltop. So, you do not know what I did to get to that hilltop. I may not know what instructions I will give to guide each of you. Therefore, you must prepare yourselves. Do you understand what I mean? These words are for your reference. In order for the Unification Church to actively operate in Asia in the future, we must create a way to travel to all countries in Asia without the approval of their governments. Do you understand what I mean? In this busy situation, when will we have time to apply for visas? When things happen without a visa, we should be able to take a plane and go and return even in one night, right? The teacher is thinking about such things.

In the future, the teacher is preparing to create a foundation for all these business areas to go out into the world centered on Asia. Therefore, in the future, our Unification Church must be able to report on the military situation of the Soviet Union and all their information about the world. Do you understand what I mean? If that happens, no investigative agency or any large country will be able to operate without us.

There may still be such things happening. Our missionaries are in the Czech Republic. They are also in China and the Soviet Union. We are laying the foundation that the Republic of Korea cannot lay. For the future of the Republic of Korea and the future of this world, we are preparing a breakthrough to penetrate into the Soviet Union in silence. We are conducting a siege operation. Transcending the nation, whether they are Germans, French, British, or Czechs, they are doing that work. Do you think this can be done with money? Just by giving orders here, they can report regardless of life or death.

The headquarters of the Japanese Communist Party is directed toward the Unification Church leader, Reverend Moon. It has not been the first time that they have featured him prominently on the front page of their official newspaper. There was a time when the highest organ of the Japanese Communist Party published such a thing, with a circulation of about 1.3 to 1.5 million copies. They made it a problem, and a fight broke out.

In this front line, even if the teacher collapses, who will push this forward? Of course, we do not know how the situation will be, but who will inherit God's heart as it is? The problem is serious. The teacher is a priest centered on this land. You are the worldwide offerings. Therefore, you must create a global economic organization centered on the teacher. Only then can your descendants and the Republic of Korea survive in the future. We must also create a global organization to realize this movement on a transnational standard. Therefore, we plan to promote international marriages in the future. The Japanese and Korean economic agents will connect with Koreans through our Unification Church. This is not done forcibly. Centered on the 30 million people of the Republic of Korea, we can inspire a high-level national ideology that they do not have, which can be called the glory of the ideal world.

President Park is holding a national unification conference centered on the Republic of Korea, but internal issues cannot be resolved centered on any nation. It cannot be made that way. Authority will not work. Politics will not work either. The issue is not about President Johnson or President Nixon of the United States. We must have the subjective authority to do this work so that we can stand before heaven.

The Unification Church needs talented people. Although there are not many of our Unification Church members in Japan, if we start nationwide activities, it will become a big problem for the Japanese Communist Party.

In the future, the foundation that can move the world will be the Republic of Korea, and among them, the headquarters church of the Unification Church in Cheongpyeong. In the future, even if they ask us to pay a thousand dollars to sleep on this floor for one night, we will fight to do so. We have taken pictures to show that we lived like this.

We must make our Unification Church members love Korea more than the members of the Korean Presbyterian Church love their holy land. We must make Christians think of Korea more than they think of the holy land of Jerusalem. Korea has many points to boast about compared to Jerusalem. The natural resources are very good.

When I went to Pyongyang to work, how much had heaven prepared? Twenty years before I met me, heaven had already made it known that they would meet someone like me in that house. The teacher went to the North at the age of 27, so heaven had been working since I was seven years old. At that time, I did not know. Could the world believe that? Many people have come out to testify about the teacher since decades ago. Those people are now testifying in front of the teacher. They are fulfilling a witness mission from the position of the archangel in relation to the teacher's path.

When God planned the creation of humanity, angels had to serve humanity, right? Did it take God a day to create humans, or did it take hundreds or thousands of years? Have you thought about this? Is it as the Christians say, that God just said, "Let there be man!" and man came out? It took hundreds or thousands of years. Until then, angels had to cooperate. When viewed from the principle of restoration and from a principled perspective, before the teacher came, those who should have cultivated a path greater than the teacher must have existed. Therefore, those who were to serve the teacher must have cooperated with the earth for centuries to lay the foundation to go out into the world of earthly Satan. Such spirits must have been serving the teacher for hundreds of years.

What is God's purpose of creation? The ultimate purpose is to use a body. To dominate the substantial world, God cannot remain as an incorporeal being; He must appear as the Father and Mother of all humankind. To stand as a subject and object that can feel stimuli with sensory organs, one must wear a body. The purpose of creation is for Adam and Eve to love each other.

When evangelism began, many people spiritually saw the teacher. It is still the same now. Therefore, the Unification Church will not perish. You, do not get tired. The more you get tired and fall, the faster the Unification Church will move forward. The teacher wants to send you abroad quickly. If you make a mistake, it will be easy to take responsibility. If you struggle abroad and survive without dying, you can stand in a position to be revered by many spiritual beings, but if you hesitate, everything will be ruined.

Now, looking back, those who have worked have all been living off the teacher. Can they go before heaven? You, the Unification Church needs talented people now. That is why we do not need many people. Centered on these results, we know that the unification front is being developed globally, and as you are in the position of the archangel, you must serve heaven with sincerity and properly carry it out. Only then can you fulfill your responsibilities and lay such a foundation.

The teacher going up to a high place called the "Shinseonbong" in Cheongpyeong is not for hunting. It is to train to become soldiers of heaven. The teacher does not go up there because there is nothing to do. There must be something that can broaden perspectives and provide insights even on such general issues.

In the future, we plan to create a movement team for the Unification Church. When we create it, the team members must not come in defeated. If they do, they should cry out in great lamentation. They must feel the sorrow of being a loser more painfully than anyone in history and cry out in great lamentation.

<Prayer> Father, we have learned through the principle what will happen to the fate of this nation and this people of thirty million in the future.
I am well aware that throughout history, countless prophets and sages have died on the path of misery, and I know that those who have drunk the bitter cup of defeat have vanished from the providential path until today. Therefore, we have come to understand that no matter how many times we fall, we must rise again. Now, we must not make the same mistakes again by reflecting on the errors of the past. We have realized the tremendous fact that we must step on the origins of those mistakes and present the conditions that allow us to remain while moving forward.

Father, although the altar of unification has walked a lonely path until today, we have not felt lonely. But how lonely must you have felt? How pitiful must your heart be, as you must include us, who are lacking and insignificant, in this immense and vast task? We earnestly hope that you will let us understand how pitiful it is for you to have to discuss this tremendous providence while holding onto us.

When I gaze at the morning sunlight, that brilliant light of glory, I want to become your son or daughter, a light of joy before you. Please grant me this. I earnestly wish to be able to cleanse all the sins that our ancestors, who were unfilial, abandoned, realizing that one cannot enter the world of your love without a strong heart.

No matter how many people there are on this earth, where is one son who can embrace your wounded heart and comfort you, and where is one daughter? There has been no one who has devoted themselves to the heavenly will for the resolution of the historical grievances of a thousand years while keeping you in mind. Although there have been those who have left wills wishing for the prosperity of countless descendants, there has been no one who has advised that this is how we must live, according to heaven's will. We know that many ancestors left blessings for their people on the path of death, but we also know that all of those wills had to fade away. Today, the groups of unification must not become such groups. Even if humanity fades away, we know that only those wills must remain for dignity to be established.

Since this is the path that humanity must traverse, we know that until now, we have been instilled with the heart to walk such a path. The Unification Church must become a sacrifice before the will of the Father. It must not become a side door. It must not become a breakthrough only needed in difficult times. It must become the main entrance that is most needed in the everyday life stage.

We must prepare the connection to be able to convey all emotional stories to you, Father. We must become a group that is determined to pass through that path more positively than anyone else, ready for the final victory before your circumstances toward the purpose.

Father, in such grace, please allow us to live and serve in such a life for even a few days. We cannot help but acknowledge that we are a group that owes a debt of ten million times. On the path where tears of sorrow intersect, we must hold onto your garment, weep, and insist that you entrust us with the remaining path of suffering, realizing that we are lacking and unable to tighten our garments. No matter how much we have devoted ourselves, we must realize that we owe too much before you and that we are too lacking.

Even if we are beaten and wounded, becoming a miserable sight with blood spilling, we have come to know that we are shameful bodies that must hide our bloodstains. Even if this body is torn and dies on the streets, we must cover it with a rag, fearing that our bodies might cause your tears, acknowledging that we are descendants of sinners who have continued for tens of millions of years.

Even if we scream for goodness until our throats burst and bleed, we must bear it and walk that path. Still, we are too lacking to resolve heaven's circumstances with our lives. Please allow us to go out with the fervor to commit our lives to join the group that remains until the end. We earnestly hope that these will come to know the immense grace that has allowed us to face such a time.

As the sun sets and the seasons change, I must burn with my heart, pondering what to offer as a gift of sincerity before heaven, struggling and worrying, unable to escape my shameful self before heaven, and discovering that I have not become a proactive person who serves you, Father. Thus, I must shed infinite tears that cannot cover my eyes. Please be with me.

Father, you are a holy being. You should not be pitiful. As the Creator, you are a symbol of authority and eternal glory, so how could you have become so pitiful? Why must you alone drink the bitter cup of defeat? We know that the reckless actions of the ancestors of humanity have ruined the history of countless ages and created the source of resentment.

This is not limited to Adam and Eve alone; we, their descendants, also carry the fallen lineage of our ancestors, possessing the same fallen nature as heirs. Therefore, we must realize that those who do not feel the trembling indignation of that fact cannot return to heaven.

Father, how much effort have you put into gathering this insignificant group of unification on the path of restoration? Please do not let your hard work become meaningless and futile, nor let us become like the sunset that loses all its light and loses its identity in darkness. Let us be a light, even if it is just a candle or a firefly, that can push back the darkness and serve as a point of discernment in one direction, for that is the mission of the unification warriors.

Thus, we must become a lighthouse and a foundation that can replace the bright sunlight of heaven, and even if we are just a stepping stone in finding that light while carrying the grievances of a thousand years, let us be a group of unification that goes forth knowing that as happiness.

Today is October 12th. I think of this day, exactly 19 years ago. I remember the time when I was worried about heaven's destiny at the crossroads of life and death. On this Sunday, corresponding to the 12th, the second Sabbath that can correspond to 120 days, please remember the children of unification scattered throughout South Korea.

Father, there are many times when you are in a pitiful position, needing to think of me and truly feel and love me. However, because it is the principle of heaven that one cannot escape the shame of having raised a wayward child and having descendants who are wayward, you know that you cannot escape from that position. If we are not worthy of your standard, you must surely awaken the next generation and send sons and daughters who will again uphold the altar of glory.

Although we are in a crowded position today, the day will surely come when heaven and earth will rejoice together in the place where the heavenly fortune welcomes us. For that to happen, we must understand that bloodstains are required as a sacrificial offering for restoration. We must know that tears can become sweat, and sweat can turn into blood on the path of restoration.

When I kneel before you, calling out to you and offering my sincerity, I must think of myself as one who is destined to draw in the heavenly connection, putting forth all my strength in the breathless and urgent moments of a woman giving birth. I cannot help but reveal my unfaithful appearance before you, Father. We have come to understand your heart, which seeks the altar of repentance with a heart of compassion.

We do not wish for you to bless us based on our own selves. We must realize that even if we shed many tears of repentance, we cannot present ourselves before you in our shameful state. How can these shameful selves call themselves your sons and how can they claim to be your family, and how can they call themselves citizens of heaven? I want to hide this body, and if there is anything that can cause this body to perish, I want it to perish. However, when we realize that you have taken responsibility for our steps and actions, let the children of unification come to know that you are a Father whom we cannot dare approach or seek closely.

We must clearly know where we should remain. You have come to find the sons and daughters of Korea. In this nation, where countless ancestors have been rejected and woven a pitiful history, you have come to this land, which is like a wasteland that cannot bear any fruit.

Today, we must realize the shame before this nation, as we, who must bear fruit in the harvest season with the reality of national reconciliation, are to be gathered.

We must follow the footsteps you have walked, day and night, without resting on this path. Even if we struggle and dedicate our lives, we must know that it is our responsibility to walk this path, even if we cannot grasp your garment or if we fall along the way, as we have been chosen before your will that has come to Korea today.

Let us become your children who lament infinitely that our arms are not broken for your purpose, that our legs are not broken, that we do not become crippled, and that our bodies do not suffer wounds.

We must continue to form a line of heavenly warriors to establish the history of national revival, and we are afraid that we may not be able to do so. Let the children gathered here understand that they are in a position to determine heaven's judgment.

Father, who called me, I confess everything before you, who has comforted my pitiful position. As I have passed through each sad day in the path of adversity, I realize how pitiful you must have felt, worrying that these would retreat and fall. Now, I must call you from that position, recognize you as my true Father, and become a child who can pray to you from that position.

Let us be a group that can take responsibility for all matters inside and outside and have the qualifications of sons without lacking.

Today, I know that the children scattered throughout the world, including Cheongpadong, are looking toward the eastern sky with tears, pursuing the final day.

If there is a child who calls out to you while struggling in the lonely and rejected journey across this beautiful land, he will surely become a friend of heaven, and heaven will draw near to him. I earnestly hope that the children of unification can welcome such a position and recognize such a life with joy.

We must clearly understand what the son you seek on the front lines of restoration is, what a family is, what the responsible figures who can represent the nation are, and what a son who can boast before the world is. If there is something to boast about in victory, let us exalt you, Father, and let us become a group that pledges to take on the shameful matters.

I entrust the entirety of this day to you, Father. Now, we must prepare once again to welcome the year 1970, so please be with us. I earnestly ask that we be equipped with the attitude to advance vigorously through the remaining three months.

Today, I ask that you grant grace in the gentle midst of every place in South Korea where people are calling out to you, and I present all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.*
